# Account Management

<a id="advanced-sorting-and-filtering"></a>
## Advanced sorting and filtering

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/advanced-sorting-and-filtering_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Advanced sort and filter functions
  - Zone sets page
  - Transport lanes page
  - Transport rates page
- Filtering
- Example filters
- Removing a filter configuration
- Sorting
- Example sort configurations
- Removing a sort configuration

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss this further, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

On select pages within CartonCloud, there is the option to utilise advanced [filtering](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Advanced+sorting+and+filtering#Advancedsortingandfiltering-filtering) and [sorting](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Advanced+sorting+and+filtering#Advancedsortingandfiltering-sorting) functionality. Simple sort functionality is still available, however, the advanced options are customisable and create a more efficient search process. This is particularly useful if you have large amounts of data to filter and sort through.

### Advanced Sort and Filter Functions

**Zone Sets page:**
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-0.png?width=670&height=234&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-0.png)
**Transport Lanes page:**
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-1.png?width=670&height=107&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-1.png)
**Transport Rates page:**
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-2.png?width=670&height=213&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-2.png)

### Filtering

To use the filter configuration function:

- Select the filter icon at the top right of the page.
- Select the field to filter by.
- Select the comparison operator to filter against.
- Enter the value you wish to compare against.
- If you wish to filter by multiple fields, select the plus icon then select the logical operator (and/or).
- Select Save.

Note, when selecting a Zone or Delivery Run to filter by a drop-down menu will appear with all available Zones and Delivery Runs you can select to filter by.

### ![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-3.png?width=446&height=143&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-3.png)

  Example Filters

**Example 1 - Zone Sets: postcodes within a range**

The below configuration is useful to find postcodes with a range (some carriers will use postcode ranges to define their income zones).
This filter will find all postcodes within the range 4200-9210.

![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-4.png?width=481&height=166&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-4.png)
**Example 2 - Zone Sets: finding a specific suburb**

The below configuration is useful to find a specific suburb.
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-5.png?width=403&height=109&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-5.png)

**Example 3 - Transport Lanes: filtering for all active Transport Lanes**

The below configuration is helpful to find all current active Transport Lanes.
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-6.png?width=421&height=117&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-6.png)

### Removing a filter configuration

To remove a filter, you have two options. You can either (a) remove filters individually using the filter configuration window or (b) remove all filters using the x in the top right corner.

![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-7.png?width=530&height=98&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-7.png)

**(a) Remove filters individually**

- Select the filter icon in the top right corner.
- You will see all the current filter configurations you have applied.
- Click the delete icon next to the filter configuration you wish to delete.

**(b) Remove all filters**

- Select the x icon next to the filter function icon to delete all filter configurations.

### ​​​​​​​Sorting

To use the advanced sort configuration function follow the below steps;

- Select the sort function icon in the top right corner.
- Select if empty values should show first or last.
- Select the field to sort by.
- Select the sort order (a-z or z-a).
- If you wish to sort by more than one column at a time, select the plus icon.
- Select Save.

![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-8.png?width=281&height=183&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-8.png)

### Example sort configurations

**Example 1 - Zone Sets: location entries without an assigned zone**
The below configuration would be utilised when you are wanting to find all Location Entries that you have not yet assigned to a Zone.
![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-9.png?width=284&height=185&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-9.png)

### Removing a sort configuration

To remove a sort configuration, you have two options. You can either (a) remove sort configurations individually using the sort configuration window or (b) remove all sort configurations using the x in the top right corner.

![advanced-sorting-and-filtering-10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/advanced-sorting-and-filtering-10.png?width=546&height=101&name=advanced-sorting-and-filtering-10.png)
**(a) Remove sort configurations individually**

- Select the sort icon in the top right corner.
- You will see all the current sort configurations you have applied.
- Click the delete icon next to the sort configuration you wish to delete.

**(b) Remove all sort configurations**

- Select the x icon next to the filter function icon to delete all sort configurations.

<a id="cartoncloud-login-options"></a>
## CartonCloud Login Options

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/cartoncloud-login-options_

### Login Options

There are multiple login options to access CartonCloud. These options include:

- Standard email and password
- SSO (WMS Premium feature only)
- Social login

### SSO

*Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).*

Enterprise [Single Sign-On (SSO)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Enterprise-Single-Sign-On-SSO) is the ability for users to log in with one set of credentials to get access to multiple corporate apps, data and websites which they have permission for. Enterprise Single Sign-On helps to strengthen security and compliance.

For more information on SSO, please see [here.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Enterprise-Single-Sign-On-SSO)

### Social Login

You can log into CartonCloud using your Google or Microsoft account. This is useful if you wish to avoid having to create another set of login credentials and use existing ones.

To log in via Google or Microsoft:

- Click the Google or Microsoft login button on the login screen.
- If your Google or Microsoft account matches an existing CartonCloud user, you will be logged in instantly.

![cartoncloud-login-options-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/cartoncloud-login-options-0.png?width=285&height=346&name=cartoncloud-login-options-0.png)

**Points to consider:**

- You still need to be invited as a user to CartonCloud to log in.
- Ensure the email you are using for your social account is the same email utilised for your CartonCloud user invite.
- If you log in with your Google account, you can no longer use your CartonCloud email and password. You will always have to use your Google login.

---

<a id="custom-field-linking"></a>
## Custom Field Linking

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/custom-field-linking_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Available field links
  - Linking a required consignment data field to a sale order field
  - Linking an address opening time to consignment data
  - Linking to a delivery address
  - Linking a transport products to consignment items
  - Linking a sale order service type to a transport service type

### Purpose

Custom fields can be linked together to allow information to be automatically transferred between multiple areas of CartonCloud.

For example, by using Custom Field linking an address can have a custom field called "Opening Time" to store the opening time for all address records in CartonCloud. By linking that field appropriately the system can then automatically populate that opening time in Consignment data. Then, whenever you book a Consignment you will be able to see what time the pick up opens.

This article will cover some examples of common custom field linking use cases. However, keep in mind these are just a small sample of the possible scenarios that can be set up.

### Available Field Links

Currently, the following custom field links are available.

- Address to Consignment Data
- Transport Product to Consignment Item
- Sale Order to Consignment Data

**Linking a required Consignment Data field to a Sale Order field**

As Sale Orders can be used to generate Consignments there is a specific requirement that when a Sale Order Custom field is linked to a Consignment custom data field that is required that it also is also set to be required. This behaviour eliminates the possibility to create a consignment that is missing data from a required custom field.

The most obvious example of this would be if a Consignment requires a Service Type, but the Sale Order record does not provide it (perhaps the packer did not fill the field in). As CartonCloud will enforce both fields to be **required** at the time of linking the custom fields, this scenario cannot occur.

**Linking an Addresses Opening Time to Consignment Data**

This example makes it possible to automatically pull through the opening time set within an Address record through to Consignments which use that Address record. This same process could also be used for a closing time if required.

To begin, navigate to the Custom Fields page by typing "Custom Fields" into **Search for Anything!**

Within the Addresses tab, select **+Add Custom Field**. Then create a custom field for the opening time as shown below.

It's important to note that the **Field Location** type needs to be set to Deliver, Collect, or Onforwarder.

Ensure the custom field is marked as **Active** and then select **Save**.

Next, navigate to the Consignment Data tab within the Custom Fields page and once again select **+Add Custom Field**. Then create a custom field for the opening time as shown below.

Pay extra attention to the **Field Location**, in the case you are following this tutorial to link a Closing Time then you would instead want to select Delivery for this option.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-field-linking-0-png.png?width=305&height=302&name=custom-field-linking-0-png.png)

Ensure the custom field is marked as **Active** and then select **Save**.

**Linking to a Delivery Address**

So far the steps have created a custom field for the collection's opening time. These next steps will show how to also set up a custom field for the opening time of a delivery address.

Within the Consignment Data tab of the custom fields page select **+Add Custom Field**.

Then create a custom field similar to the below. Choose your own preference for **Required** and **Show on Mobile**.

Once completed, select **Save**.

Now, navigate back to the Address tab and edit the address custom field you previously created.

Turn on Field Mapping and then in **Link this field to**, select the Consignment Data custom fields you have created as shown below.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-field-linking-1-png.png?width=383&height=448&name=custom-field-linking-1-png.png)

Select**Save**, and the custom fields will be linked.

Now, you will need to populate the Opening time custom field within your addresses record.

To do this, navigate to the Address record you want to set an opening time against. Select **Edit** and then enter in the time that the address opens. Then scroll to the bottom of the page and select **Save**.

Once completed, whenever you use that address within a Consignment the opening time will automatically pull through to the Consignment's data.

**Linking a Transport Products to Consignment Items**

For this scenario, we will use the example of linking the DG Class of a [Transport Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Transport+Products) to a Consignment Item when a Consignment is booked.

To begin, navigate to the Custom Fields page by typing "Custom Fields" into **Search for Anything!**

Navigate to the Transport Products tab and select **+Add Custom Field**. Then select create a Custom Field like the below using the name you prefer (some may prefer shortening it to "DG Class").

Ensure the custom field is marked as **Active** and then select **Save**.

Next, navigate to the Consignment Items tab within the Custom Fields page and once again select **+Add Custom Field**. Then create a custom field for the Dangerous Goods class as shown below.

Also, making this field "Required" and "Shown on Mobile" is completely optional. Most will choose to not make this required in case an item they are sending is not DG.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-field-linking-2-png.png?width=316&height=569&name=custom-field-linking-2-png.png)

Ensure the custom field is marked as **Active** and then select **Save**.

Now, navigate back to the Transport Product tab and edit the DG Class custom field you previously created.

Turn on Field Mapping and then in **Link this field to**, select the Consignment Item custom field you have created.

Select**Save**, and the custom fields will be linked.

Now, you will need to populate the Dangerous Goods Class custom field within your Transport Product record.

To do this, navigate to the [Transport Product](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Transport+Products) record you want to set a pallet type against. Select **Edit** and then enter in the Pallet type in the field. Then select **Save**.

Once completed, whenever you use that Transport Product within a consignment as a consignment item the Dangerous Goods Class will automatically pull through to the consignment items data.

**Linking a Sale Order Service type to a Transport Service Type**

This example is only relevant if you are [generating consignments from Sale Orders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Generating+a+Consignment+from+a+Sale+Order).

By linking a Sale Order Custom field to the Consignment Data custom field called [Service Type](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Service+Types) it is possible to select what transport Service Type you wish for a Sale Order to go out on. This data will then automatically populate**at the time a consignment is generated from the Sale Order**.

To begin, navigate to the Custom Fields page by typing "Custom Fields" into **Search for Anything!**

Navigate to the Sale Order tab and select **+Add Custom Field**. Then select create a Custom Field for Transport Service Type (or Consignment Service Type if you prefer this name) such as the example in the image below.

This custom field mirrors the Service Types that are already set up. The Service Types you enter will depend on what you have set up for your transport operation. To check your Service Types, navigate to the Consignment Data tab, and check the custom field named Service.

Whether the field is Required, Shown on Mobile and Shown in Heading is also optional.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/custom-field-linking-3-png.png?width=406&height=691&name=custom-field-linking-3-png.png)

Ensure the custom field is marked as **Active** and then select **Save**.

Next, navigate to the Service Type tab within the Custom Fields page and edit the custom field named Service.

Now within the field turn on Field mapping and link it to the field you just created as shown below.

Making this field "Required" and "Shown on Mobile" is completely optional and a matter of preference.

Select**Save**, and the custom fields will be linked.

Now when creating a Sale Order you will have the option to choose what the Service Type is on the Consignment which is generated from the Sale Order as shown below.

<a id="dashboard"></a>
## Dashboard

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/dashboard_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Widgets
  - Available widgets
  - How to add a widget
  - Rearrange widgets
  - Remove widgets

### Purpose

The Dashboard gives you an overview of information tracked by CartonCloud. In addition, you can select which widgets (different information) you would like displayed on your Dashboard.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/dashboard-0-png.png?width=3316&height=1712&name=dashboard-0-png.png)

### Widgets

**Available Widgets**

| **WIDGET** | **Description** | **Administrator** | **Customers** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| General Info |  | Yes | No |
| Total Consignments for last 7 days | Retrieves the number of consignments for the week.   Cached for 10 minutes, updated every 5. | Yes | Yes |
| Undelivered Consignments today | Retrieves the total of delivered/undelivered consignments for the current day.   Cached for 10 minutes, updated every 5. | Yes | Yes |
| Sale Orders History | Shows Sale Order processing performance over a 7-day scale.   Data is cached for 10 minutes, updated every 5, and is Warehouse-specific.   The data includes only Packed statuses (Packed, Dispatched). | Yes | Yes |
| Warehouse Capacity | Retrieves a breakdown of warehouse capacity by Single/Bulk pallet locations. **Blue:** Bulk/Single Pallet Locations Total   **Green:** Bulk/Single Pallet Locations Empty   **Red:** Bulk/Single Pallet Locations In Use | Yes | No |
| Invoicing |  | No | Yes |
| Customers Pallet Count | Visualises pallet occupancy over multiple weeks. Defaults to 8 weeks.   Data cached for 10 minutes, updated every 6, Warehouse-specific.   Calculated by existing POPs, new POPs and Storage information. | No | Yes |
| Containers Arrival/Departure Dates | Provides a comprehensive calendar view of container movements, tracking both incoming and outgoing containers specific to the current Warehouse. The dates are tracked using configurable custom fields, and the data calculated based on the dates found in the custom fields selected as the arrival and departures date fields. | Yes | No |
| Automation | Provides an overview of automation efficiency, tracking the percentage of automated processes over a 4 week period.   Data is cached for 10 minutes, updated every 5, and is Warehouse-specific.   The data tracks automated vs manual processes, providing a percentage of those operations that were automated. An “automated process” is defined as one which was completed without manual intervention or direct human involvement, and this data is derived from Consignment processing and Sale Order handling | Yes | No |
| Latest Releases | To help you stay up to date with new CartonCloud features and improvements.  This widget displays the most recent product updates so that you can see what’s new without leaving your workspace. The update will link to the full release log, where you can read more. | Yes | Yes |

**How to add a Widget**

- Navigate to the Dashboard page, More>Dashboard.
- Select the **cog** icon in the top left corner.
- By default, all widgets will be enabled. To disable a widget, untick the select box.
- Select **Add**to save the changes.

**Rearrange Widgets**

To change the order in which the Widgets are arranged:

- Select the cog icon in the top left corner.
- Using the Order column, adjust the numbers against the widgets accordingly.
- Click **Save**.

**Remove Widgets**

To remove widgets from the Dashboard:

- Select the cog icon in the top left corner.
- Untick the widget you wish to remove.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/dashboard-3-png.png?width=1723&height=339&name=dashboard-3-png.png)

- Click Save .

---

<a id="deletion-logs"></a>
## Deletion Logs

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/deletion-logs_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Video overview
- Step by step guide
- Filter Options Explained

### Purpose

The Deletion Logs allow you to see when a Sale Order, Purchase Order, Consignment, Manifest, Invoice, or Run Sheet has been deleted and who deleted the order.

The deletion log records clear after 60 days.

### Video overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/qpEgXBfT23A

### Step-by-step guide

- Type Deletion Logs into the Search for anything bar.
- Use the below filter options to find the order you are looking for or use the All tab and scroll through the orders.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-09-2026-08-33-21-0830-PM.png?width=670&height=116&name=image-png-Mar-09-2026-08-33-21-0830-PM.png)

- Select the log you want to view; this will display the details of the deleted record.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-09-2026-09-02-39-4877-PM.png?width=670&height=149&name=image-png-Mar-09-2026-09-02-39-4877-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-09-2026-09-03-21-7539-PM.png?width=670&height=251&name=image-png-Mar-09-2026-09-03-21-7539-PM.png)

### Filter Options Explained

- **Model** – Filter by record type: Sale Order, Purchase Order, Consignment, Manifest, Invoice, or Run Sheet.

Note: The Invoice dropdown option and Invoice deletion log entries are hidden from Administrator users who have “Hide all charging information” enabled.

- **Search by ID / Reference / User / Customer** – Quickly locate a specific record using its unique identifier or associated details.
- **User** – See deletions performed by a specific user.
- **Date Deleted** – Find deletions within a specific time frame.

---

<a id="demo-account"></a>
## Demo Account

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/demo-account_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Accessing the demo account and contacting CartonCloud
- Contact CartonCloud
- Samples
- Sample sale orders (iOS only)
- Barcode cheat sheet
- Sample push notifications
- Drop-down notifications
- Notification list
- Available functionality
  - Limitations / what is different

### Purpose

The CartonCloud mobile apps offer users without an existing CartonCloud account the option to explore the mobile apps at their leisure. Using the demo account login, users have access to all the functionality that the CartonCloud apps offer, on a limited set of sample consignments.

### Accessing the Demo Account and Contacting CartonCloud

The Demo Account can easily be accessed from the app's login screen.

Select the Demo account button at the bottom of the screen and you will be logged in to the demo account.

Any information entered into either the "*Email"* or "*Password"* field will be disregarded upon selecting the Demo Account button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-0-png.jpeg?width=273&height=486&name=demo-account-0-png.jpeg)

You will then be prompted to select a User mode. Each user modes documentation is linked below to assist. For more information on switching user modes see the article:

User Modes

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-1-png.jpeg?width=268&height=477&name=demo-account-1-png.jpeg)

Once logged in as the Demo user, the slide-in menu (activated by the menu button in the top-left position on the navigation bar) will display "Demo User" as the user name.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-2-png.jpeg?width=273&height=486&name=demo-account-2-png.jpeg)

### Contact CartonCloud

Throughout the app, while logged in as the Demo user you will notice "*Contact CartonCloud*" buttons at the bottom of your screen. These buttons do not appear in the app when a "normal" sign-in is used. They are simply provided for the Demo Account to facilitate interested new users to contact the CartonCloud team.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-3-png.jpeg?width=269&height=479&name=demo-account-3-png.jpeg)

Upon selecting any of the contact buttons, you will be presented with several options - either call CartonCloud directly or email us, or alternatively request to be contacted by entering your contact details.

| ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-4-png.jpeg?width=750&height=1334&name=demo-account-4-png.jpeg) | **![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/demo-account-5-png.jpeg?width=750&height=1334&name=demo-account-5-png.jpeg)** |
| --- | --- |

### Samples

A set selection of consignments is provided for the Demo Account. These have been chosen to represent various different types of consignments possible in CartonCloud.

You will notice a mixture of standard Delivery, Pickup, Onforwarder and Point-To-Point jobs - some with Cash On Delivery (COD) options, some with Blank Proof of Delivery (POD) options etc.

On every refresh of consignments within the Demo Account. the consignments will be completely reloaded, independent of whether jobs have been previously completed within the app. The selection of sample consignments is not only based on their types but also their locations. Assuming the user has given the app access to their current location, consignments in a major city near the current location will be chosen. If no location access has been granted (or you find yourself in the middle of the Outback, a long way away from any major city), consignments from a random city will be loaded.

### Sample Sale Orders (iOS only)

A set selection of sale orders is provided for the Demo Account while operating in Picking mode.

**For more information on how to switch user modes, check out this article: [User Modes](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/User+Modes)**

**For more information on how Scan Picking works, check out this article: [Scan Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Scan+Picking)**

On every refresh of sale orders within the Demo Account. the sale orders will be completely reloaded, independent of what packing status they are currently in.

### Barcode Cheat Sheet

To enable you to make the most of Picking mode, we have compiled a "cheat sheet" containing barcodes for the warehouse locations and products used in the Demo account.

Please find the PDF for download below:

[CartonCloud_Demo_barcode_cheatsheet_v1.pdf](https://help.cartoncloud.com/download/attachments/47775852/CartonCloud_Demo_barcode_cheatsheet_v1.pdf?version=1&modificationDate=1496383776000&api=v2)

### Sample Push Notifications

In order to introduce new users to the way that CartonCloud handles Push Notifications, sample Push Notifications are provided within the Demo Account.

**Want to know more about how Push Notifications work in CartonCloud? Check out this article: [Push Notifications](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Push+Notifications)**

### Drop-Down Notification

On login into the Demo Account, a sample drop-down Push Notification will be displayed after a certain amount of time (1 min) has passed.

### Notification List

Every time the consignment list is refreshed, a number of random notifications will be generated and displayed in the *Notifications* view which can be accessed via the slide-in menu.

### Available Functionality

All standard functionality is available for users of the Demo Account. As a demo user you will still be able to submit PODs and Invoice Photos, lodge errors, optimize your route, group consignments, pack sale Orders etc.

**Please check out "*Limitations / What is Different*" below for information on a few things that are handled differently for the Demo Account.**

As mentioned previously it is important to note that all consignments will be completely reloaded on refreshing the consignment list, dropping all changes you have made previously.

**Limitations / What Is Different**

- **POD / Invoice Photo / Error Uploads:**PODs, Invoice Photos and Errors can be generated as normal and will be submitted to the server as per the standard app behaviour. Please note though that these uploads will be dropped by the server upon receiving them from the Demo Account, meaning they won't be stored in CartonCloud.
- **Push Notifications**: Unlike standard accounts, the demo account is not registered to receive Push Notifications from the CartonCloud web app as changes are made to relevant consignments. Please see above ("*Sample Push Notifications*") on how to still get a taste for how CartonCloud handles Push Notifications within the mobile apps.
- **Failed Uploads:** While failed uploads will be shown in the Outbox as per standard behaviour, they will be deleted upon refreshing the consignments, as all consignments are reloaded in their original state.
- **Job Allocation:**The Job Allocation features is disabled in Demo mode. For more information on how this feature works, check out this article: [Job Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Job+Allocation)
- **Picking & Packing / Sale Orders:**The demo account can go through the same steps as a standard account when packing Sale Orders - start packing, pack (by scanning or manual entry), finish packing. Please be aware though that unlike a normal account, the demo account will not save the progress of a Sale Order that is currently being packed and will reload Sale Orders as "Awaiting Pick & Pack" once you leave the packing view.

---

<a id="enterprise-single-sign-on-sso"></a>
## Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/enterprise-single-sign-on-sso_

### Table of Contents

- What is Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO)
- How to enable Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) for your CartonCloud account
- How to log into CartonCloud using Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO)
- How to set up Single Sign-On (SSO) for your company

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

### What is Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO)

Enterprise Single Sign-On (SSO) is the ability for users to log in with one set of credentials to get access to multiple corporate apps, data and websites which they have permission for. Enterprise Single Sign-On helps to strengthen security and compliance.

If you don't already have Single Sign-On and would like to configure it please see [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#how-to-set-up-single-sign-on-for-your-company)for some useful tips.

### Prerequisites for Single Sign-On

To enable Single Sign-On for CartonCloud login you need to already have Single Sign-On set up for your company. If you do not already have Single Sign-On set up for your company and would like to do so please find the below information:

- Single Sign-On can be set up using an existing account such as Google Workspaces or Microsoft.
- Here is an article that guides you through setting up Google as the SSO provider.
- Here is an article that guides you through setting up Microsoft as the SSO provider.

### How to enable Enterprise Single Sign-On for your CartonCloud account

Enterprise SSO is a WMS Premium only feature. For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### How to log into CartonCloud using Enterprise Single Sign On (SSO)

Please ensure the email address you use for your SSO is the same email address set up for your CartonCloud user.

- From the login screen, click Sign in with Enterprise SSO.

![enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-0.jpeg?width=623&height=327&name=enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-0.jpeg)

- Enter the **Provider ID**. This will depend upon your organisations SSO provider.

![enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-1.jpeg?width=611&height=415&name=enterprise-single-sign-on-sso-1.jpeg)

- Depending on your SSO Provider, the login screen will vary. Enter your SSO login details.

<a id="how-to-reset-your-cartoncloud-connect-password"></a>
## How to reset your CartonCloud Connect Password

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-reset-your-cartoncloud-connect-password_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to reset your CartonCloud Connect Password

### Purpose

To reset your CartonCloud Connect password. See [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Printing-from-CartonCloud) for more information on printer and CartonCloud Connect setup.

Please note that your CartonCloud Connect password is **different**to your CartonCloud app password.

### How to rest your CartonCloud Connect Password

NOTE: Your password for CartonCloud Connect is different from your password for CartonCloud itself.

If you need to reset your password please follow the below steps (you must have Administrator permissions to CartonCloud to complete the below steps).

- Type in Organisation Settings in the Search for anything bar at the top of the application.
- Select the Features & Options tab within Organisation Settings.
- In the Printing Configuration section, click the Reset Password button.
- A screen will be displayed showing the email address and a randomly generated password you need to enter into CartonCloud Connect.

<a id="how-to-write-a-cartoncloud-support-case"></a>
## How to write a CartonCloud support case

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/how-to-write-a-cartoncloud-support-case_

🛠️ How to Write a Support Case That Gets Results

Want quicker answers and fewer follow-up emails? A well-written support case helps our team resolve your issue faster and more accurately.

Here’s what to include when submitting a case to [CartonCloud Support](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket):

---

### ✅ What to Include in Your Support Case

- 🔢 **Reference Numbers**
Include any relevant order, invoice, consignment, or product numbers.
- 🔗 **Links**
Add direct links to the specific orders, products, customers, or screens you're referring to in CartonCloud.
- 📝 **Clear Description + Expected Outcome**
Explain what’s going wrong, where it's happening, and what you expected instead. The more specific, the better.
- 🚨 **Error Messages**
If there’s an error message, copy and paste the exact wording into your case.
- 👤 **User, Customer, or Warehouse Details**
Let us know if the issue is tied to a particular user, customer account, or warehouse.
- 🔌 **Integration Details**
If an integration is involved (e.g. Xero, Shopify, WooCommerce):
  - Tell us which system is connected
  - Include the relevant order or reference number
  - Briefly explain what the integration should be doing (e.g. syncing orders, updating tracking)
- 🖼️ **Screenshots or Screen Recordings**
Visuals are extremely helpful. Attach screenshots or a short screen recording if you can.

---

### 🚀 Why It Matters

Providing this information up front means:

- 🔁 Less back and forth
- ⏱️ Faster investigation and resolution
- 🎯 Better outcomes for your business

---

### ✍️ Example Support Case

**Subject:** Support Request: Storage Charge Error – Unable to Finalise Charges (Storage Period 1110 / Invoice 956)

Hi Support Team,

When attempting to finalise charges for **Storage Period 1110** on **Invoice 956**, I receive the following error message:

**Income: No General Per Pallet Qty rates loaded**

I am receiving this error in the **City Warehouse** and **here is a direct link to the storage period**.

This error is blocking the invoicing process for the period. Based on the setup, I expected the system to apply the correct storage rates and allow the charges to be finalised without issue.

Could you please review and advise on how to resolve this issue so I can proceed with invoicing?

**I’ve attached a screenshot**for reference showing the error message on screen.

Let me know if you need any further information.

Best regards,

---

<a id="introduction-to-custom-fields"></a>
## Introduction to Custom Fields

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/introduction-to-custom-fields_

### Table of Contents

- What are Custom Fields
- How to add a Custom Field
- Field Descriptions
- Field Types

### What are Custom Fields

Custom Fields allow you to record specific information against different records within CartonCloud. For example, you might want to record the Container Number on a Purchase Order or the Carrier Consignment Note on a Sale
Order.

Note, if you are looking for information on how to use Custom Fields through the API, please see: [Custom Fields in the API](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Fields+in+the+API)

### How to add a Custom Field

- Navigate to the Custom Field page by typing **Custom Fields** into the Search for anything bar.
- From here, you can select what record you would like to add a Custom Field to by selecting the relevant tab.

![Custom_Fields_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Custom_Fields_1.jpeg?width=670&height=89&name=Custom_Fields_1.jpeg)

- Once you have selected the correct tab, click +Add Custom Field .

![Custom_Fields_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Custom_Fields_2.jpeg?width=670&height=151&name=Custom_Fields_2.jpeg)

- Using the below Field Descriptions, fill in the relevant information for the Custom Field.

![Custom_Fields_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Custom_Fields_3.jpeg?width=457&height=453&name=Custom_Fields_3.jpeg)

### Field Descriptions

| **Field** | **Description** | **Required to create Custom Field** | **Default** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name | Name of the Custom Field. It will be visible on tables, export files and forms for the entity of Custom Field. | Yes | empty |
| Short Name | Short Name of Custom Field. It can be used in different tables and export files. | No | empty |
| Map Field Name | The Map Field Name maps columns from imported files to the entity. This field is not editable.  Example: For a custom field named "Reference" for entity "Container", its map field name can be "reference", so that whenever a file is imported for the Container, if it contains a column "reference", it will map to "Reference" custom field for Container. | Yes |  |
| Field Type | Defines the type of Custom Field (refer to the table below, **Types of Custom Fields**) | Yes | Text |
| Field Mapping (toggle) | Once enabled, [Field Mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Custom+Field+Linking)allows you to create a link between two custom fields so that when data is entered in one custom field, it is pulled through to another. For example, if you had a Custom Field for Opening and Closing Times against the address and Consignment, you could link the fields so that the opening and closing times for an address will show against the Consignment. | No | Un-checked |
| Options |  |  |  |
| Required (toggle) | With this enabled, the Custom Field will be required against the record. This means the field must be filled when adding or editing the record. | Yes | Checked |
| Internal Use Only (toggle) | With this enabled, the Custom Field will not be visible to external users (Customer and onforwarder users); only admin, packer and driver users will be able to see the custom field. This setting is helpful if you want to store sensitive information such as carrier expenses or other internal data from your customers. **Note that you can NOT have the required setting enabled with this setting enabled.** | No | Un-checked |
| Display |  |  |  |
| Show on Mobile | Custom Field will appear in the CartonCloud Mobile app (both iOS and Android) | Yes | Checked |
| Show in Headings | With this selected, you will have the option to add this custom field as an available field in the list view for that custom field. For example, if you add a Sale Order Custom field and select 'Show in Headings', you can configure the Sale Order list view to include the custom field as a heading. See [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignments) (under the heading Configuring the Consignments List View) for more information on how to edit the list view. |  |  |
| Show on Sort Arrivals | This Custom Field will appear on the manifest "Sort Arrivals" screen when enabled. | No | Unchecked |
| Active / Enabled (toggle in top right corner) | With the toggle enabled, the Custom Field will be active and visible for the entity. If disabled, this field will not appear for the entity. |  |  |

### Field Types

| **Type** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Integer | The custom field will accept whole numbers only without decimals. |
| Decimal | The custom field will accept both numbers and decimals. |
| Text | The custom field will accept both text and numbers. |
| Date | The custom field will accept dates only. On clicking DateTime Custom Fields, a calendar will automatically popup to select the date. |
| Boolean | Custom Field will act as a dropdown with only two options, "Yes" and "No". It helps do checkbox type actions.   When selected in the "Add/Edit Custom Field" page, a field called "Default Custom Field Option" will define the default option for this type of custom field. |
| Drop Down Only available on the following custom field types,   Address   Consignment Data   Consignment Item   Sale Order   Transport Product | The custom field will act as a dropdown with predefined options. With this option selected, a field called Drop Down Option will appear, allowing the user to define options from the dropdown box.  These fields can then be reordered by dragging and dropping the dropdown option and repositioning it as required. The order of the fields will be reflected in the other areas of the system which use those custom fields, for example, when adding a new consignment.  **Dropdown Default Value** If none is specified, you can define which value you want the dropdown to use in the Default field.  This is particularly useful for the Consignment Data "Service" custom field, as it allows you to define what service a consignment should use by default, including when a [consignment is generated from a Sale order](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Generating+a+Consignment+from+a+Sale+Order). |

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/gORdnvkCrKY

<a id="multi-factor-authentication-mfa"></a>
## Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/multi-factor-authentication-mfa_

### Table of Contents

- What is Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)
- Factors to consider before enabling Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)
- How to enable Multi Factor Authentication (MFA) on the web app
- How to enable Multi Factor Authentication (MFA) on the mobile app

### What is Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)

Multi Factor Authentication forces the user to provide an authentication code (from their authentication app of choice) each time they log in. This provides greater security and account protection.

### Factors to consider before enabling Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)

- You can not use MFA if you are already using SSO.
- MFA can be enabled at the individual user level, and is up to the individual user to enable this feature themselves, unless Enterprise Security is enabled and MFA usage is enforced across all users in the account. Please see Organisation Settings - Security for more information.
- Once MFA is enabled, you will always need to provide an authentication code from your chosen authentication app each time you log into the web and mobile CartonCloud app.
- You will need an authentication app of choice to be able to access the authentication code. One Authentication app includes Google Authenticator, however, there are a number of different options to choose from.
- It is recommended that you choose and download an authenticator app (if you do not already have one) to your mobile device before you set up MFA for your user.
- It is recommended that once you enable MFA, you log out of all sessions on all browsers/computers/mobile apps everywhere (other than the one being used to set up MFA, which forces a logout).

### How to enable Multi Factor Authentication (MFA)

- From within your CartonCloud account, click your account name in the top left corner and select Dashboard. This will take you to the My dashboard page. This is information relevant to your individual user not the CartonCloud account.

![MFA_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_1.jpeg?width=670&height=337&name=MFA_1.jpeg)

- Under the My Settings section, select Change My Settings .

![MFA_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_2.jpeg?width=670&height=352&name=MFA_2.jpeg)

- Under the Multi Factor Authentication heading, click Manage MFA .

![MFA_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_3.jpeg?width=670&height=356&name=MFA_3.jpeg)

- Set up MFA on your authentication app using the QR code or the secret.
- Enter the authentication code.

![MFA_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_4.jpeg?width=670&height=356&name=MFA_4.jpeg)

- Your user will now be set up with MFA and be required to enter an authentication code each time you log into either the web or mobile app.

### How to enable Multi Factor Authentication (MFA) on the mobile app

If you do not access the web app and need to enable MFA from your mobile app you can follow the below steps.

- Within the mobile app select Settings from the side navigation bar.
- Toggle Multi-factor Authentication .

![MFA_5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_5.jpeg?width=190&height=384&name=MFA_5.jpeg)

- You will then need to either copy the secret to your authenticator app or can follow the click through button to your authenticator app.

![MFA_6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/MFA_6.jpeg?width=194&height=395&name=MFA_6.jpeg)

- You will then need to enter the code from your authenticator app.

---

<a id="notification-emails"></a>
## Notification Emails

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/notification-emails_

### Table of Contents

- What is Notification Emails
- Warning when using Notification Emails
- Available Notification Emails
- How to set up Notification Emails

### What is Notification Emails

CartonCloud allows you to set up email notifications for your customers and also your internal staff. From the Notification Emails page you can set up internal notifications and from the Customer Settings you can set up customer email notifications. See [Configuring Outgoing Notification Emails to Customers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers)for steps on how to set up customer email notifications.

### Warning when using Notification Emails

Please note when using these notifications that every customer will be included in each notification. Therefore, it is highly recommended you only include company internal emails and NOT customers.

### Available Notification Emails

| Notification | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Sale Order Successfully imported (via Parser) | When a Sale Order is successfully imported (applies for every customer) via a parser |
| Purchase Order Successfully imported (via Parser) | When a Purchase Order is successfully imported (applies for every customer) via a parser |
| Sale Order Approved (by customer) | When a Sale Order is approved by a Customer from their login (applies for every customer) |
| Purchase Order Approved (by customer) | When a Purchase Order is approved by a Customer from their login (applies for every customer) |
| Manifest Approved (by customer) | When a Manifest is approved by a Customer from their login (applies for every customer) |
| New Consignment Error Created Notification (Filtered) | When a consignment error is recorded (for every customer) |
| Awaiting Stock Sale Order now available | When a Sale Order moves from "Awaiting Stock" to "Awaiting Pick and Pack" |

### How to set up Notification Emails

- Navigate to Notification Emails by typing Notifications into the Search for anything bar and select Notification Settings.
- Click +Add Email Address .

![Notification_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Notification_1.jpeg?width=670&height=130&name=Notification_1.jpeg)

- Enter the Name and Email and click Create .

![Notification_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Notification_2.jpeg?width=498&height=302&name=Notification_2.jpeg)

- Tick the relevant notification you would like the email address to receive.

![Notification_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Notification_3.jpeg?width=670&height=189&name=Notification_3.jpeg)

- Click Save .

<a id="notifications"></a>
## Notifications

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/notifications_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to action notifications
- Configuring notifications

### Purpose

Notifications allow you to keep on top of admin tasks within CartonCloud. Notifications are located on the Dashboard page.

### How to action notifications

- Against the notification you wish to view/action click the blue hyperlinked number.
- This will take you through to the page where you can view the items that need action.

**Notification Explanations**

| **Notification** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- |
| Unpacked Sale Orders | All Sale Orders that are in 'Awaiting Pick and Pack' status. |
| Draft Invoices | All Invoices that are in a 'Draft' status. |
| Draft Bills | All Bills that are in a 'Draft' status. |
| Unallocated Address Strings | Address strings that need to be allocated. |
| Unallocated Consignments | Undelivered Consignments that are not yet allocated to a Delivery Run. |
| Unassigned Consignment Documents | Consignment Documents that are not yet assigned to a Consignment. |
| Unassigned Sale Order Customer Invoices | Sale Order Customer Invoices that are not yet assigned to a Sale Order. |
| Unallocated Delivery Runs | Delivery Runs that do not have a Driver allocated to them. |
| Unallocated Delivery Runs (Today & Earlier) | Delivery Runs for either today or earlier that do not have a Driver allocated to them. |
| Unallocated Delivery Runs (Next Day) | Delivery Runs for tomorrow that does not have a Driver allocated to them. |
| Address Requiring Geocoding | Addresses that have not been geocoded. |
| Incoming Purchase Orders | Purchase Orders that have been added to CartonCloud but have not yet been received. |
| Booked Manifests | Manifests that have been booked. |
| Unallocated, Undelivered Consignments | Consignments that have not been allocated to a driver or delivered. |
| Unassigned A2IC Consignment Mappings | Consignments that have not been assigned to [A2IC mapping](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-Address). |
| Unresolved Consignment Errors | Consignments that have been marked with an error. |

### Configuring notifications

To select which notifications you wish to be displayed:

- Select the cog in the top right of the Notifications widget.
- Tick the Notifications you would like to be displayed.
- Select Save .

<a id="reordering-the-consignment-purchase-order-and-sale-order-list-view"></a>
## Reordering the Consignment, Purchase Order and Sale Order list view

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/reordering-the-consignment-purchase-order-and-sale-order-list-view_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to manually reorder the orders in the last view

### Purpose

When using the CartonCloud mobile app, you have the ability to manually reorder the order the Consignments, Purchase Orders and Sale Orders appear in the list view.

### Benefits

- Enables the user to sort orders/jobs according to their preference without the sort order getting lost upon refreshing the job list.
- Allows the user to choose how they would like the orders/jobs to appear, making it easier for them to complete their work.

### How to manually reorder the orders in the list view

- Navigate to either the Putaway, Picking or Delivering mode.
- You will see the applicable orders listed.
- Hold down on the relevant order and drag it to the position in the list you wish it to be.

<a id="reset-cartoncloud-password"></a>
## Reset CartonCloud Password

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/reset-cartoncloud-password_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to reset your CartonCloud password from the Login Page
- How to reset your CartonCloud password from your Dashboard

### Purpose

If you have forgotten your CartonCloud login password, you can reset it from the CartonCloud login page or from your Dashboard.

### How to reset your CartonCloud password from the Login Page

- From the CartonCloud login screen, click I forgot my password .

![Reset Password_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Reset%20Password_1.png?width=670&height=353&name=Reset%20Password_1.png)

- Enter your email address and you will receive an email prompted you to reset your password.

### How to reset your CartonCloud password from your Dashboard

- When logged in, navigate to your Dashboard by opening the menu arrow beside your account name.

![Reset Password_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Reset%20Password_2.webp?width=670&height=114&name=Reset%20Password_2.webp)

- Click "Change My Settings"

![Reset Password_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Reset%20Password_3.webp?width=670&height=305&name=Reset%20Password_3.webp)

- Check the "Change Password" box, this will open the password fields.

![Reset Password_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Reset%20Password_4.png?width=670&height=293&name=Reset%20Password_4.png)

- Enter new matching password in both fields, save.

**Remember:** A password needs to have at least 8 characters and should include at least one upper case letter, one lower case letter, one number, and one special character. Can't remember complex passwords? We recommend using a password manager.

<a id="retrying-documents"></a>
## Retrying Documents

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/retrying-documents_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- More information on retrying documents
- Viewing retrying documents
- Manually retrying documents
  - To perform a manual retry from the documents page
  - To perform a manual retry while viewing an individual document

### Purpose

Retrying documents have been uploaded to CartonCloud, but the Customer Reference Number on the document can not be matched to any order in CartonCloud. This process prevents documents from being categorised as 'Unassigned' straight away and allows time for the corresponding order to be added to CartonClud.

### More information on retrying documents

Documents are uploaded via Email, FTP, or manually uploaded to CartonCloud. The Parsers extract the **Customer Reference Number** from an invoice. CartonCloud then uses this **Customer Reference Number** to try and automatically assign the Invoice to the correct Consignment, however in some cases, the Consignment Customer Invoices is imported before the Consignment. To prevent the Invoices from immediately going to "Unassigned", they're put into a "Retrying" status while waiting for the associated Consignment to arrive.

If a Consignment Invoice is uploaded to the system **before** the actual Consignment, a **Consignment Customer Invoice** is created with a **Retrying** status. This Retrying status means that the system will automatically look for the Consignment that the Consignment Invoice belongs to and then link them together if it does find it. If the system does not find the correct Consignment on a retry, it stays in retrying and checks again every hour. The retrying process will continue for **24 hours**. If no Consignment is found that matches the Consignment Invoice, then it stops retrying and becomes an **Unassigned** Consignment Invoice.

### Viewing retrying documents

You can view documents that are in a retrying status by:

- Navigating to the Documents page, **More**>**Documents**.
- Select the **Retrying** tab.

![Retrying Document_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Retrying%20Document_1.avif)

### Manually retrying documents

There are two ways to retry a Document in Retrying status manually. You can do so from either the Documents page or directly within the individual document.

**To perform a Manual Retry from the Documents page:**

- Select which Document(s) you would like to retry by ticking the check box next to the relevant Documents.
- Click **More**.
- Click **Retry**.

**To perform a Manual Retry while viewing an individual Document:**

- Click on the relevant Document.
- Click on the **Retry** link in the Actions **row**.
- Click **Ok** in the prompt that appears to confirm the Manual Retry.

---

<a id="solving-missing-email-notifications-and-creating-a-catch-all-email"></a>
## Solving missing Email Notifications and Creating a catch all Email

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/solving-missing-email-notifications-and-creating-a-catch-all-email_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Setting up an email account to receive all notifications
- CartonCloud email settings

### Purpose

Occasionally there can be instances when customers report that they haven't received an email notification from CartonCloud. The root cause of this issue could be many things such as a company's email firewall or spam filters.

To get one step closer to diagnosing the problem we suggest tenants set up a catch-all email so they can view all emails sent from CartonCloud to their customers.

By following this article you can set up a process to see what is being sent to your customers and confirm the date & times that emails were sent.

### Setting up an email account to receive all notifications

There are two options you can use for setting up an email account,

1. Set up a new email account within your own company email service (note, this address may attract a large volume of emails which can easily use up available space).
2. Use Google to set up a Gmail account for your business (Gmail has the capacity to hold a large volume of emails). To use this option you can follow this guide to setting up a Gmail account .

### CartonCloud Email Settings

- Once the email address you wish to use is set up you will need to navigate to Organisation Settings by selecting More in the main menu, followed by Organisation Settings .
- Once there select the Email tab.
- Add the new catch-all email address to the field Email addresses to receive all customer emails (Separate by ";" or ",")
- You will now receive a copy of all outbound notifications from CartonCloud to this email address.
- This is also a great way to view what is being sent to a customer and confirming that files are being attached and viewable.

---

<a id="suppliers"></a>
## Suppliers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/suppliers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Overview
- Use cases
- Video explainer
- Adding a supplier

### Purpose

Please note if you are using the latest version of CartonCloud (accounts created after 1 July 2019, the below functionality is only available for the warehouse system, not transport (drivers/carriers). If you have any questions, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

Suppliers are like Customers but used for Bills rather than Invoices. Suppliers are typically contractors you have working for you who you pay, or freight companies and Onforwarders you use.

### Overview

Suppliers themselves are neither Drivers nor Carriers, they're simply an intermediate layer which can connect multiple Drivers and/or Carriers to specific Customer Charges.
Suppliers need to be linked to Drivers and/or Carriers, allowing CartonCloud to build bills for Consignment that those Drivers/Carriers have delivered.

The following diagram provides 3 examples of the ways Suppliers can be connected:

![Suppliers_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Suppliers_1.jpeg?width=670&height=232&name=Suppliers_1.jpeg)

### Use Cases

**Transport**

- You have a driver working for you as a contractor who charges the same rates always
- You have a driver working for you as a contract who charges different rates depending on which customer he is delivering
- You have multiple drivers working for you but they are part of one subcontracted company, and you pay a single bill for all of their work

**Warehouse**

- You pay the Warehouse Provider for storing / pick pack, and they charge you the same rate for all of your clients
- You pay the Warehouse Provider for storing / pick pack, and they charge you different rates for each of your clients
- You need to construct individual bills per-customer within a single warehouse.

### Video Explainer

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/_qh2XHJjyAg

### Adding a Supplier

- To create a supplier, first, select Contacts in the main menu, then select Suppliers from the drop-down.
- Now, select Add Supplier and fill in the details for the supplier you are using (Suppliers can be Drivers, carriers, onforwarders, or 3PL Warehouses)
- If your CartonCloud account has multiple warehouse locations you can also select which warehouses will be using this Supplier.

![Suppliers_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Suppliers_2.jpeg?width=325&height=304&name=Suppliers_2.jpeg)

- Once completed, select Add Supplier and it will be created in the system.
- Now once Viewing the Supplier, select Edit to set up some further details.
- The first tab is for the Basics. From this tab, we can link which Supplier Charge (Expense Customer Charge/Rate Card) the supplier is to be linked to.
- Setting up Customer Charges / Rate Cards for a Supplier is a simple process of entering how much the Supplier charges for its service.
- As Customers may have different rates with a Supplier it is also possible to add multiple supplier charges. For example, in the screenshot below, all Customer's will be charged the "Driver Rates Based on 60%" except for Bobs Grocery which will be charged the "Bob's Grocery 2018 Rates".
- It is important to note that the Supplier Charges are not what the Customer will be invoiced from CartonCloud - that is always determined by the Rate Card / Customer Charge set against the Customer. This is explained further in Rate Cards Overview . Instead, Supplier Charges are used to track the expense of a service completed by a Supplier.

![Suppliers_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Suppliers_3.jpeg?width=388&height=284&name=Suppliers_3.jpeg)

- The Bill tab allows you to set up when the suppliers next bill date will be, how often that billing cycle repeats, as well as set up an Accounting Connector to automate the invoicing process.
- The Email tab allows you to set up emails to receive notifications regarding this specific supplier.
- The Warehouse tab allows you to edit which Warehouses use the supplier (as you saw when initially setting up the Supplier)
- The Barcode tab is an advanced setting which should only be used with the assistance of CartonCloud Support .
- Finally, the Linked to Tab all is where you can set Suppliers to be either a Carrier, Driver or Warehouse. In the example below, we have Tony's Transport being added as a Carrier.
- You can have multiple drivers linked to one supplier. An example would be if Tony's Transport supplies multiple rigid trucks with drivers they can all be linked to one supplier which would supply one weekly / monthly bill.

---

<a id="adding-a-comment-to-an-address"></a>
## Adding a comment to an Address

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-a-comment-to-an-address_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- How to add a comment to an address on the web app
- How to add a comment to an address on the mobile app

### Purpose

To add a comment against an Address that is visible on the web app and mobile app for other users. You can add a comment to an address from both the web app and mobile app.

### Benefits

This is useful for drivers delivering to the address as they can then record important delivery information for future deliveries.

### How to add a comment to an address on the web app

- Navigate to the Address page, More > Addresses .
- Select the Address you wish to add a comment to.
- Select the Comments tab.

![adding-a-comment-to-an-address-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-an-address-1.png?width=670&height=341&name=adding-a-comment-to-an-address-1.png)

- Click Add comment .

![adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2.png?width=268&height=554&name=adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2.png)

- Write the comment.
- Click Submit .
- This comment will now appear against the address on both the mobile app and the web app.

### How to add a comment to an address on the mobile app

- Open the Consignment.
- Click the comments button against the address.

![adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2.png?width=289&height=598&name=adding-a-comment-to-an-address-2.png)

- Type in the comment
- ![adding-a-comment-to-an-address-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-an-address-3.png?width=279&height=603&name=adding-a-comment-to-an-address-3.png) Click **Post**. ![adding-a-comment-to-an-address-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-a-comment-to-an-address-4.png?width=249&height=539&name=adding-a-comment-to-an-address-4.png)
- The comment will now appear against the address in the mobile and web app for all users.

<a id="adding-and-editing-an-address"></a>
## Adding and editing an Address

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-and-editing-an-address_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to add an address
- How to edit an address

### Purpose

When you add an address in CartonCloud, it will be available for selection when creating a Consignment or Sale Order. If the address doesn't already exist in your account, you can also add the address whilst you are creating the Consignment or Sale Order.

### How to add an address

You can add an address individually, or you can do so in bulk. To edit or add addresses in bulk, please see [this](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Bulk-Import-Addresses) page.

To add an address individually:

- Navigate to the Addresses page , and type Addresses into the Search for anything bar.
- Click +Add Address .

![adding-and-editing-an-address-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-and-editing-an-address-0.png?width=670&height=88&name=adding-and-editing-an-address-0.png)

- You can either fill in the fields manually or use the Company name to search for the address. When searching for the address, the form will auto-populate with information gathered from Google.
- If you enter a email address against the address a POD will be automatically sent to this address when a Consignment is delivered to the address. If you wish to send this POD to two email addresses ensure you seperate the address with ;
- To disable the POD email notification, navigate to the Customer Settings under the email notifications and disable the POD notification.

![adding-and-editing-an-address-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-and-editing-an-address-1.png?width=302&height=531&name=adding-and-editing-an-address-1.png)

- If using the auto-population feature, be sure to double-check that the resulting address is accurate.
- Click Add Address , and the address will be added to the system.

Once created, you will arrive on to the View Address page for that address. From here, further actions can be taken using the address. For more details, see the [View Address](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/View+Address) article.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/741PtUmQEWM

### How to edit an address

- Navigate to the relevant Address by typing Address into the Search for anything bar.
- Click on the relevant Address.
- Scroll down and click Edit against the actions bar.

![adding-and-editing-an-address-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-and-editing-an-address-2.png?width=670&height=326&name=adding-and-editing-an-address-2.png)

- Make the relevant changes and click Save .

<a id="address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated"></a>
## Address not appearing on a new Sale Order or Consignment (Unallocated)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- The solution - assigning the address string

### Purpose

It is possible when importing orders using a parser or integration that the new order will be created without an address record appearing. Instead, the address will simply show as Unallocated. An example of this can be seen below.

This most commonly occurs when the address used on the import file is missing key address fields such as Suburb or Postcode, or they are misspelt.

![address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-0.png?width=431&height=256&name=address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-0.png)

### The Solution - Assigning the Address String

- To assign the address string to an address record, while viewing the Sale order, select the Allocate link. You will be taken to the Allocate tab of the address string's page.

![address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-1.png?width=562&height=218&name=address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-1.png)

Now either:

1. Allocate it to an existing address record or
2. Allocate it to a new address record

- Once the address record is chosen, select Allocate .
- Navigate back to the Sale Order by going to the Sale Orders tab of the address string, finding it the Sale Order, then selecting View
- The address record that was selected will now appear.

![address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-2.png?width=577&height=273&name=address-not-appearing-on-a-new-sale-order-or-consignment-unallocated-2.png)

<a id="addresses-in-cartoncloud-address-strings"></a>
## Addresses in CartonCloud (Address Strings)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/addresses-in-cartoncloud-address-strings_

### Table of Contents

- What are Address Strings
- Allocating Address Strings
- Introduction to Addresses

### What are Address Strings

Most WMS/TMS systems allow for a different address to be recorded for the same location multiple times. The problem with this is when you book a delivery to a location with multiple addresses you have to guess which address is accurate.

In CartonCloud we've solved this problem using Address Strings. You can think of Address Strings as an alias for the actual address in the system's address book.

When orders are entered into CartonCloud a new address will be created, however, if the address matches a current address you will be prompted to allocate the address to the existing address (this new address will become an address string).

![addresses-in-cartoncloud-address-strings-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/addresses-in-cartoncloud-address-strings-0.png?width=407&height=359&name=addresses-in-cartoncloud-address-strings-0.png)

For example, in the diagram above, imagine each Address String has been created by a customer entering a new order. In CartonCloud, once you allocate each Address String to the correct system address, the address string will always point to it from that point on.

In the example provided you can see how this would be beneficial as sometimes details are incorrect, such as the spelling in Address String 2, or incomplete, like street details in Address String 3.

Once these three address strings have been allocated to the address in the system, the delivery will always be marked with the correct address when those address strings are used.

When inputting an address for the first time make sure the address follows the below format:

Company Name, Street, Suburb, Postcode, State

If you do not provide at a minimum the street name and postcode, CartonCloud will request you to allocate the address to an address string.

If an address with an existing Address String is imported with either a completely new or updated email and/or telephone number, then the Address String will be updated with the changes.

### Allocating Address Strings

For information on how to allocate an Address String please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Address-not-appearing-on-a-new-Sale-Order-or-Consignment-Unallocated).

### Introduction to Addresses

This video covers the basics of Addresses in CartonCloud including how to create them. We suggest following along with the video to create a few Addresses of your own within your CartonCloud tenancy.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/741PtUmQEWM

Timestamps

- 0:00 - Adding an Address
- 1:13 - Address Email (Sending PODs to the Address)
- 1:44 - Address Geocoding
- 2:52 - Merging Addresses
- 3:40 - Starring an Address
- 4:12 - Address Comments
- 5:13 - Address Strings
- 6:29 - Bulk Importing Addresses

**Next step: [Introduction to Custom Fields](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Introduction-to-Custom-Fields)**
