<a id="organisation-settings-warehouse"></a>
## Organisation Settings - Warehouse

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/organisation-settings-warehouse_

### Table of Contents

- [Sale Orders Configurations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#sale-orders-configurations)
- Consignment / Warehouse Fulfilment
- [Purchase Order Configurations](https://help.cartoncloud.com#purchase-order-configurations)
- [Cross Customer Picking](https://help.cartoncloud.com#cross-customer-picking)
- [Display Location Warnings](https://help.cartoncloud.com#display-location-warnings)
- [Replenishment Configuration](https://help.cartoncloud.com#replenishment-configuration)
- Pack Screen

### Sale Orders Configurations

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Default Sale Order Pick List Format | The style of the Sale Order Pick List that's exported, picking from either pre-built templates or customisable templates: Default XLS Format - pre-defined excel sheet template which shows each Sale Order Product on its own line Default PDF Format - select this format if you wish to set your own customer [Document Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Document+Templates) |
| Sale Order Statuses on which  overriding pre-existing Sale Order (or deleting an existing Sale Order) is allowed | When importing a Sale Order via Parser (see: [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers)), by default a duplicate Sale Order (same reference) will only override an existing Sale Order if the Sale Order is Rejected. However, the statuses which allow overriding can be configured here. By enabling other statuses, Sale Orders in those statuses will be overwritten if another file is imported with the same Reference (and for the same customer). When a Sale Order is overwritten, it will be deleted from the system, and a new Sale Order will be created with the updated details to replace it. For example: Sale Order ID 145 exists in the system and is in a rejected status. A new Sale Order is parsed in with an identical reference number. Sale Order with ID 145 is then deleted and a new sale order is generated using the parsed in data, it is assigned a new ID by the system. |
| Mobile App Configuration | **Regex for Tote Barcode Validation:**see [Pick to Tote](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Pick-to-Tote) for more information.  **Allow Forceful Completion of Individual Sale Orders**: this setting controls the behaviour on the mobile app for orders that are not part of a Wave Pick. If this setting is turned ON, it will allow warehouse staff using Picking and Picking (Lecacy) to pack order without first having to re-scan all products.  **Enforce Strict Process:**Packers will be required to first scan a location, then a product to confirm its quantity. They can not simply select a product from the Sale Order's product list and confirm its quantity. *See: [Enforce Strict Processes For Packing And Putaway](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Enforce+Strict+Processes+For+Packing+And+Putaway)* **Enforce Adhoc Charges before completing Pick:** by enabling this setting, the adhoc charges screen will show before completing the pick and will prompt you to record any adhoc charges if necessary. Please note, this is currently in Beta release and is only available to Android users. Please reach out to the team via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport) to have this feature enabled. |
| Consignment / Warehouse Fulfilment | **Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order:**   **TMS & WMS CartonCloud Accounts:**   No    Yes, when a new Sale order is packed only   Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pack Completion     **WMS Only CartonCloud Accounts:**         **No** - no Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will be generated  **Yes, when Sale Order is Picked Only** - a Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will generate when a Sale Order is picked.  **Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pick Completion** - a Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will generate when a Sale Order is imported or upon pick completion.       **Populate Consignment Items Data from a Sale Order:**   *When CartonCloud creates Consignment Items from Sale Order Products (SOPs), the system does not consider pallet IDs or warehouse locations. Instead, CartonCloud uses:*     *The quantity on each SOP,*   *The **Product Packaging Product Unit of Measure**(PPPUOM) and its conversion rates, and*   *Whether a Transport Product is mapped to each PPPUOM.*     *Two setting options control how SOP quantities are converted into Consignment Items:*    **Yes - Use Product Unit of Measure**: CartonCloud processes each SOP **individually**, one at a time:         For each SOP, quantities are examined from largest PPPUOM to the smallest. If that PPPUOM has a mapped Transport Product, CartonCloud creates a Consignment Item for it. The remaining quantity is then reassessed using the next PPPUOM. If a Consignment Item for the same mapped Transport Product already exists, its quantity increases instead of creating a duplicate. If a PPPUOM does not have a mapped Transport Product (e.g., Pallet), a Consignment Item is not created for it.    **Yes - Aggregate into Optimal Unit of Measure**: The total quantity across all SOPs for each Warehouse Product is calculated, then the process from the above option is run on the aggregated totals of each Warehouse Product rather than each SOP.        **Copy Sale Order Customer Invoices to Consignment:**      Use Organisation Settings No  Yes |
| Sort Pick/Pack List by Warehouse Locations Pick Order | Within CartonCloud it is possible to create an order within your Warehouse Locations that you wish to pick Sale Orders by. This requires you to update the pick_order field on each Warehouse location to assign it a numbered order in respect to all other locations that you wish to pick it by.  Products will then display on Sale Orders in the order where the first row is the Warehouse Location with the lowest pick_order number when compared to all other warehouse locations on the Sale Order. To do this, you need to enable the Sort Pick/Pack List by Warehouse Locations Pick Order setting.  **For more information:** [Setting up Warehouse Locations Pick Path Sequence](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-warehouse-locations-pick-path-sequence) |
| Show Custom Fields on Sale Order Products | Custom Fields can be set up for Products. This setting allows you to control if they show on Sale Order Products or not.    In addition, it enables the use of Sale Order Product Custom Fields in the API. |

### Consignment / Warehouse Fulfilment

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Automatically Generate a Consignment from a Sale Order | *This setting is turned on by default and will enable the [Pack Screen](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Pack-Screen) workflow for all customers. If you wish to turn it off for certain customers, you can do so from the [Customer Settings - Warehouse Management (Sale Order Tab).](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Warehouse-Management)* **No** - no Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will be generated  **Yes, when Sale Order is Picked Only** - a Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will generate when a Sale Order is picked.  **Yes, on Sale Order Import or Pick Completion** - a Consignment ([Warehouse Fulfilment](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Types-Warehouse-Fulfilments)) will generate when a Sale Order is imported or upon pick completion. |
| Copy Sale Order Customer Invoices to Consignment | **Yes** - if there is a Sale Order Customer Invoice is loaded against the Sale Order, and a Consignment is created from the Sale Order, this invoice will transfer over to the Consignment.  **No** -  if there is a Sale Order Customer Invoice is loaded against the Sale Order, and a Consignment is created from the Sale Order, this invoice will NOT transfer over to the Consignment. |

### Purchase Order Configurations

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Default Purchase Order Verification List Format | The style of the Purchase Order Verification that's exported, picking from either pre-built templates or customisable templates:   **Default XLS Format**: Pre-defined excel sheet template which shows each Consignment on its own line   **Default PDF Format:**Select this format if you wish to set your own customer Document Templates. |
| Purchase Order Statuses on which overriding pre-existing Purchase Orders allowed on upload. | When importing a Purchase Orders via Parser (see: [Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Parsers)), by default a duplicate Purchase Order (same reference) will only override an existing Purchase Order if the Purchase Order is Rejected. However, the statuses which allow overriding can be configured here. |
| Mobile App Configuration | **Prevent Purchase Orders from being verified if unconfirmed quantities exist:** Stops warehouse staff from being able to verify a purchase order as entered the warehouse if it contains unconfirmed product quantities. By default, this is possible and automatically confirms the product quantities with their current values, even if that means confirming a product with quantity 0. **Enforce Strict Process:**Warehouse staff will be required to first scan a product, then proceed with either verifying or allocating the scanned product. In the case of allocation, this requires either a location scan or a manual location search. In the case of verifying, the product quantity needs to be confirmed. See: [Enforce Strict Processes For Packing And Putaway](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Enforce+Strict+Processes+For+Packing+And+Putaway) **Enforce Adhoc Charges before completing Receiving:** by enabling this setting, the adhoc charges screen will show before completing receiving and will prompt you to record any adhoc charges if necessary.  **(Android Only) Present Ad hoc Charges Before the Locate Screen:** with this setting enabled, the charges tab of a Purchase Order will present itself prior to the locate tab. With this setting disabled the charges tab will display after the locate tab. |

### Cross Customer Picking

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Allow adding any customers stock to any Sale Order | Cross customer picking allows Any Product (regardless of Customer) to be added to Any Sale Order. For example, if you have two Customers and each has one Product:   Customer A → Leg of Ham   Customer B → Balloons Normally, CartonCloud would prevent you from creating a Sale Order for Customer B and adding a Leg of Ham to it.   However, by turning on Cross Customer Picking you're enabling this functionality.   With Cross Customer Picking, any Product can be added to Any Sale Order. |

### Display Location Warnings

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Display a warning message on Verification screen when stock is allocated to a non-empty location | With this setting enabled, a warning message will appear on the verification screen when stock is allocated to a location that is not empty |

### Replenishment Configuration

| **Setting** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Replenishment Report Logic | Select the report logic you wish to use from the Replenishment Report Logic drop-down menu. This will determine the quantity you are are replenishing by.  Default: standard replenishment logic which uses the Replenishment Quantity Configuration settings defined at the Product level  Overstock from Sale Order demand: uses the default report logic and will look at the level of stock required for Sale Orders in awaiting pick and pack status and will conduct an over replenishment to compensate for these Sale Orders. When running the Replenishment, the report will highlight if the move is for stock relating to a Sale Order in pick and pack status or not |
| Advanced Replenishment Configuration |  |
| Sale Order Allocation Pick Face Quantity Depletion Limit (%) | If you wish to apply a limit to the quantity of product picked from a pick face for a Sale Order, apply a percentage in the **No Limit** text bar under **Sale Order Allocation Pick Face Quantity Depletion Limit.** |
| Replenishment Stock Allocation Status | Select the **Replenishment Stock Allocation Status**you wish to use. This will determine what stock is being used to replenish the pick face locations.       **Onhand:**uses all stock in the warehouse, including stock currently allocated to a Sale Order (only for orders that have not been picked or packed yet). This is useful as it will help move stock that is already allocated to a Sale Order into pick face locations, ready for when the order needs to be picked. Note, it is strongly advised if you are using this setting not to process Sale Orders for that product whilst conducting the Replenishment.    **Free:**only includes stock available in the warehouse and is not allocated to a Sale Order. It is advised you use this status if you are planning to process Sale Orders while conducting the Replenishment, as the stock allocated to a Sale Order will not be utilised to replenish the pick faces. |
| Use Last Allocated Location for Minimum Trigger | When enabled, any product without a pickface assigned will use the last allocated location instead of all pickface locations for the minimum trigger. This reduces redundant replenishment tasks for products without a pickface and simplifies stock management by focusing on the most relevant location. |

### Pack Screen

| Hide Auto-Generated Consignment Items | If Auto-Generated Consignment Items will be hidden or not on the Pack Screen. For more information, please see [here](https://cartoncloudorg.lightning.force.com/articles/Knowledge/Mapping-Product-Unit-of-Measures-to-Consignment-Fields-Transport-Products) |
| --- | --- |

<a id="organisation-settings-white-labelling"></a>
## Organisation Settings - White Labelling

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/organisation-settings-white-labelling_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Considerations
- How to customise White Labelling

Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport).

### Purpose

White Labelling allows you to provide a seamless brand experience within the CartonCloud application for your organisation and your customers. With White Labelling you can customise your warehouse web app design by choosing to update the header with your own logo and select the background colour (white or blue).

### Considerations

- White Labelling is a WMS Premium only feature. For more information on WMS Premium and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team here .
- Changes made at the White Labelling settings will be applied for all users.
- Only Admin users have the ability to access and make changes to White Labelling.

### How to customise White Labelling

- Navigate to the Organisation Settings, More > Organisation Settings .
- Select the White Labelling tab.

![White Label_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/White%20Label_1.png?width=670&height=357&name=White%20Label_1.png)

- From here you can customise the app header logo and the colour theme of the app header.
- Notice that changes made will instantly be applied to offer you a preview of what the changes will look like in the application. Only once you select save will the changes be applied.
- For the logo, the logo you have selected as the Organisation default will be applied here. Click Customise Logo if you wish to upload a logo or change the current logo you have set up.

![White Label_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/White%20Label_2.png?width=670&height=353&name=White%20Label_2.png)

- This will take you to the Organisation tab on the Organisation Settings. Select Upload Logo or Override Logo (if you already have a logo selected) to select the logo you wish to apply. Keep in mind the logo you select should have a transparent background so that it works with the colour background selected.

![White Label_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/White%20Label_3.webp?width=670&height=356&name=White%20Label_3.webp)

<a id="organisation-settings-basics"></a>
## Organisation Settings Basics

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/organisation-settings-basics_

Organisation Settings in CartonCloud are the settings which directly relate to *your company*. Every CartonCloud tenancy should configure these as part of their setup.

To navigate to the **Organisation Settings** page, either type "Organisation Settings" in the Search for anything bar or in the main menu click on **More**, then in the drop-down menu select **Organisation Settings**.

At this stage of the setup, many of these settings are not required to be changed, so for now only complete the first three tabs: **Organisation**, **Address**, and **Email**.

If you need further assistance completing these tabs navigate to the [Organisation Settings Per Page support article](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Organisation+Settings) which provides further details on what each setting does.

Remember that these details will be used on documents and email notifications when your tenancy becomes operational. So it is important that they are accurate.

We will return to the remaining tabs later on in the setup.

![Org Settings_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Org%20Settings_1.webp?width=670&height=395&name=Org%20Settings_1.webp)
Next step: [S](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530055347)[etting up Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Setting+up+Users)

---

<a id="tms-settings-bulk-export-import"></a>
## TMS Settings Bulk Export/Import

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/tms-settings-bulk-export-import_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Exporting TMS settings

### Purpose

To update the TMS settings against your customers in bulk there is an option available via the Customer List page to export all of your customers' TMS settings to a CSV file, which you can then open in excel, modify and then import the updates back into CartonCloud. This can be very useful when you want to change a TMS setting across some or all of your customers in bulk.

### Exporting TMS settings

- To export the file, click on Contacts > Customers then click the Related button, and select Export Customer TMS Settings .
- A CSV file will be downloaded. Once downloaded, open the CSV and make changes to the relevant settings that you wish to update.
- Once changes are made to the CSV file, ensure you Save it before proceeding further
- To import the file back into CartonCloud, click the Related button again and select Import Customer TMS Settings , select the updated file and your Customer settings will be updated.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/2b3AT32dzy4

# Account Management > Printer Setup

<a id="configuring-multiple-printers"></a>
## Configuring Multiple Printers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/configuring-multiple-printers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Prerequisites
- Steps on how to configure multiple printers with CartonCloud
- Configure printers to multiple warehouses
- Printer match conditions

### Purpose

If you need to use multiple label printers, you will need to add the printer to your printer setup with CartonCloud.
You can have a different printer for each warehouse in CartonCloud.

### Prerequisites

- Ensure the default printer is enabled. To do this, follow the below steps:
  - Navigate to Organisation Settings ( More > Organisation Settings ).
  - Select the Features & Options tab.
  - Check Enable Zebra Label Printing via CartonCloud Connect (Printnode).
  - Select a default printer from the Remote Printer drop-down.

![configuring-multiple-printers-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-0.png?width=670&height=219&name=configuring-multiple-printers-0.png)

### Steps on how to configure multiple printers with CartonCloud

- Navigate to **Print Log** (**More**>**Print Log**)
- Click Configure Printers .

![configuring-multiple-printers-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-1.png?width=670&height=99&name=configuring-multiple-printers-1.png)

- Click Add Printer Configuration .

![configuring-multiple-printers-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-2.png?width=670&height=110&name=configuring-multiple-printers-2.png)

- Fill in the fields.

![configuring-multiple-printers-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-3.png?width=670&height=399&name=configuring-multiple-printers-3.png)

- Click Save .

### Configure printers to multiple warehouses

The default printer set at the Organisation Settings will be applied to all of your warehouses (if you have more than one). If you would like to set a different default printer for each warehouse you need to ensure you set up a different printer in each warehouse with printer match conditions (printer match conditions are explained in greater detail below) that allow that printer to be selected instead of the default one. To do this, you need to set the printer to the specific warehouse:

- Navigate to the relevant warehouse.

![configuring-multiple-printers-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-4.png?width=670&height=108&name=configuring-multiple-printers-4.png)

- Select More > Print Log .
- Click Configure Printers.
- Click Add Printer Configuration .
- Ensure all fields are left as Any.
- Select the printer you wish to make the default for this warehouse.
- Because all fields are left as Any , the printer for this warehouse will now be the Remote Printer you have configured.

![configuring-multiple-printers-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/configuring-multiple-printers-5.png?width=670&height=248&name=configuring-multiple-printers-5.png)
Each printer configuration is warehouse specific, meaning you need to be in the applicable warehouse when setting up your printer configurations. The warehouse you are in when setting up the printer configuration will only be available in that warehouse, therefore, if you wish to make a printer available in each warehouse you will need to configure the printer in each warehouse.

### Printer match conditions

When determining what printer to use, CartonCloud will look for matches between the printer configuration and the order (that the label is being printed for). CartonCloud will use the order of priority and scoring system (below) to determine which match/s persists if there is more than one match.

**Order of priority in which a printer is selected:**

| Match | Points |
| --- | --- |
| Customer | 16 |
| Modal | 8 |
| User | 4 |
| Type | 2 |
| Print Format | 1 |

Examples:

| **Match** | **Printer A** | **Printer B** | **Printer C** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Customer | Sunshine Drink Bottles | Coastal Coffee Company | Any |
| Modal | Sale Order | Consignment | Consignment |
| User | Sam | John | Sam |
| Type | Label | Any | Any |
| Print Format | zpl | Any | Any |

**Example 1: Sam is printing a zpl label for a Sale Order for Coastal Coffee Company = Printer B**

Printer A = Model (8), User (4), Type (2), Print Format (1) match = 15 points
Printer B = Customer (16) = 16 points
Printer C = User (4) = 4 points

**Example 2: Sam is printing a Consignment zpl label for Sunshine Drink Bottles = Printer A**

Printer A= Customer (16), User (4), Print Format (1) = 21 points
Printer B = Model (8) = 8 points
Printer C= Model (8), User (4)= 12 points

**Example 3: John is printing a Consignment zpl label for any other customer = Printer B**

Printer A= Type (2), Print Format (1) = 3 points
Printer B = Model (8), User (4) = 12 points
Printer C = Model (8) = 24 points

**Example 4: Any user is printing a Purchase Order label for any other customer**

Fallback to the default printer in Organisation Settings.

Making the most of your ZPL printer with Tony's Tips:

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/ORvjvwuFr3M

---

<a id="label-printers"></a>
## Label Printers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/label-printers_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Mobile label printer and desktop label printer
  - Mobile label printers
  - Desktop label printers
- Setting up printers with CartonCloud Connect
- Printer DPI Requirements
- Label Sizes

### Purpose

When selecting the appropriate label printer for your operation it is important to consider what your operational requirements are and what type of printer can best meet these needs. There are two types of label printers to choose from, a mobile label printer and a desktop label printer.
**Please note, to auto-print from the CartonCloud mobile app your printer must be capable of ZPL command language.**

### Mobile Label Printer and Desktop Label Printer

| **Factors to consider** | **Mobile Label Printer** | **Desktop Label Printer** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Direct print from both CartonCloud Web and Mobile App | Yes | Yes |
| High volume of labels | No | Yes |
| Easy install and configuration | Yes | Yes |
| Portable | Yes | No |

**Mobile Label Printers**

Mobile label printers are portable printers that can be carried by the user whilst completing their work. The Mobile Label printer connection must be WIFI and not Bluetooth to be able to print with CartonCloud (see [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Printing-from-CartonCloud) for more information on how to connect your printer).

| **Mobile Label Printer** | **Tested with CartonCloud** | **Notes** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Brother RJ4250WB | Yes |  |
| Zebra ZQ521 | Yes | Not compatible with MacBook or MAC Desktops |

**Desktop Label Printers**

Desktop label printers are designed for high-volume label printing, however, are not portable and will remain stationary.

| **Desktop Label Printers** | **Tested with CartonCloud internally** |
| --- | --- |
| Brother TD-4550DNWB 300dpi Direct Thermal Label/Receipt Printer | Yes |
| Zebra ZD420D | Yes |
| Zebra ZT230 | Yes |
| Zebra ZT400 | Yes |
| Bixolon XD3-40D | Yes |

### Setting up Printers with CartonCloud Connect

For information on **setting up your printers** with CartonCloud please see [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/technical-information/printing-from-cartoncloud-printer-setup).

For specific information on **Label Printing** with CartonCloud please see [Label Printing](https://help.cartoncloud.com/kb2/technical-information/printing-from-cartoncloud-printer-setup/label-printing).

### Printer DPI Requirements

For reliable label output:

- Use Zebra printers with consistent DPI across all label printing stations — we recommend 203 DPI.
- Avoid mixing 203 DPI and 300 DPI printers in the same environment.
- If you must use 300 DPI printers, ensure they are configured to emulate 203 DPI mode (refer to your printer’s documentation).
- CartonCloud labels are optimised for 203 DPI output and may not render correctly on higher DPI settings without additional setup.

### Label Sizes

For **Pallet (POP) Labels** and **Consignment Labels**, the 100x150mm Direct Thermal Labels are compatible with the printers mentioned above (This can also be 101x149mm).

For **Wave Pick Labels,**102 x 74mm labels are compatible with the printers mentioned above.

<a id="label-printing"></a>
## Label Printing

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/label-printing_

### Table of Contents

- Label Printing with CartonCloud Link to Label Printing with CartonCloud
- Label Printing Workflow Link to Label Printing Workflow
- How to set up label templates
- How to set up label printing
- Printing to PDF
- Printing to PDF settings
- Direct print via CartonCloud Connect
- How to print labels from the mobile device
- How to print labels from the mobile app

### Label Printing with CartonCloud Link to Label Printing with CartonCloud

There are two ways to print labels with CartonCloud; you can either [**export to PDF**](https://help.cartoncloud.com#printing-to-pdf) or [**direct print to a label printer**](https://help.cartoncloud.com#direct-print-via-cartoncloud-connect) (ZPL language) via CartonCloud Connect.

You can print Purchase Order, Sale Order and Consignment labels.

### Label Printing Workflow Link to Label Printing Workflow

**Sale Order**

![label-printing-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-0.jpeg?width=670&height=169&name=label-printing-0.jpeg)

**Purchase Order**

![label-printing-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-1.jpeg?width=670&height=169&name=label-printing-1.jpeg)

**Consignment**

The Consignment label can be printed on the web app at any stage.

### How to set up label templates

You can set up your label templates from either the Organisation Settings level or the Customer Settings level. At the Organisation level, the template will apply to all customers; however, if you set the template up at the Customer level, it will only apply to that particular Customer.

Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Document-Templates) for steps on how to modify your label templates.

### How to set up label printing

You can print your labels either by **exporting to PDF** or **printing them directly to a label printer**via CartonCloud Connect.

### Printing to PDF

All labels can be exported to PDF from within CartonCloud and be printed from your computer using your computer's printer configurations.

Positives of printing to PDF

- Easy to set up.

Limitations of printing to PDF

- Not as seamless/efficient as printing directly to a label printer using CartonCloud Connect.
- Can only print PDF from the web application (cannot be performed from the mobile device).

### Printing to PDF settings

When printing to PDF, there are two different ways to generate the labels, either as 4-per-page (suitable for printing to A4) or single-label-per-page (suitable for printing to a label printer).

You can configure the way that labels are generated on a per-customer basis from within the Customer Settings:

- Navigate to the relevant Customer.
- Click **Edit**.
- Select the **Transport Management** tab.
- Scroll down to the **Labels** section.
- Select the **PDF Label Page Type**.

![label-printing-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-2.jpeg?width=464&height=133&name=label-printing-2.jpeg)

- Select **Save**.

### Direct Print via CartonCloud Connect

Please note that to be able to print directly to a label printer, you must have a label printer capable of handling ZPL language. Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Label-Printers) for information about label printers.

To print directly to a label printer, you must use CartonCloud Connect. Please click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Printing-from-CartonCloud) for steps on how to set up CartonCloud Connect.

Positives of direct print

- Can print from the mobile device
- Enables a more efficient and seamless process as you can print whilst picking and packing on the warehouse floor

Limitations of direct print

- Require a label printer capable of handling ZPL language. Click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Label-Printers) for information about label printers.

### How to print labels from the mobile device

**Scan Move**

- After scanning a Warehouse Location or Purchase Order Product.

![label-printing-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-3.jpeg?width=229&height=495&name=label-printing-3.jpeg)

- Upon moving a Purchase Order Product.

![label-printing-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-4.jpeg?width=222&height=480&name=label-printing-4.jpeg)

**Purchase Orders**

- Upon verifying/receiving a **Purchase Order**.

![label-printing-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-5.jpeg?width=247&height=534&name=label-printing-5.jpeg)

### How to print labels from the web app

**Purchase Orders**

- Upon verifying/allocating the **Purchase Order**.

![label-printing-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/label-printing-6.jpeg?width=670&height=310&name=label-printing-6.jpeg)

- At any stage from the **Products** tab on the **Purchase Order**.

**Sale Orders**

- At any stage from the **Details** tab on the **Sale Order**.

**Consignments**

- At any stage from the **Details** tab on the **Consignment**.

<a id="remote-print-jobs"></a>
## Print Log

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/remote-print-jobs_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to use the Remote Print Jobs screen
- Understanding computer and printer status
- Configure Printers
- Troubleshooting printing issues

### Purpose

The Print Log screen gives a history of all attempted print jobs. This allows you to troubleshoot why jobs may have not printed or to verify jobs were printed successfully. In addition, you can configure printers from this page.

### How to use the Print Log screen

Attempted print jobs will show on this page with the below information:

![Print Log_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Print%20Log_1.jpeg?width=670&height=99&name=Print%20Log_1.jpeg)

| Column heading | Description |
| --- | --- |
| PrintJob Id | The Id reference of the print job |
| Created | The data the print job was created |
| Title | Title of the document being printed |
| Entity | The entity in CartonCloud the job is being printed from. |
| Printer | The printer being utilised for the print job and the status of the printer when the computer was last connected.   **Offline**: this means the last time the printer was connected is not online and will not be able to print. You will need to check the printer is connected to your computer and is turned on.  **Online**: this means the last time the computer was connected to the printer, the printer was online. |
| Computer | The computer being utilised for the print job and the status of the computer if it is connected to CartonCloud Connect:  **Offline**: the computer is not connected to CartonCloud Connect, you will need to connect it in order to be able to print. Please see [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Printing-from-CartonCloud) for more information.  **Connected**: the computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect and should be working as expected. If it is still not printing when it reads as Connected there must be another issue, please read the other checks. |
| Warehouse | The warehouse that the print job was generated from |
| State | The status of the print job e.g done |

### Understanding computer and printer status

The below combinations of computer and printer status will help you when trying to troubleshoot printing issues:

| **Computer status** | **Printer status** | **What does this mean** | **Steps to resolve** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Connected | Online | The computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect and the printer is online | Print jobs should be printing as expected. If they are not please see [Troubleshooting Printing](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Troubleshooting-Printing) for troubleshooting steps |
| Offline | Online | The computer is not currently connected to CartonCloud Connect and the last time it was connected, the printer was online. | Print jobs will NOT be printing as the computer needs to be connected to CartonCloud Connect. See  [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Printing-from-CartonCloud) to connect your printer. |
| Connected | Offline | The computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect and the printer is offline. | Print jobs will NOT be printing as even though the computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect, the printer is offline. Ensure the printer is turned on and is connected to the computer that is connected to CartonCloud Connect (the one mentioned in the print job). |
| Offline | Offline | The computer is not connected to CartonCloud Connect and the last time it was connected the printer was online. | Print jobs will NOT be printing as the computer is not connected to CartonCloud Connect and the printer is offline. Ensure the computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect, see  [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Printing-from-CartonCloud). And that the printer is turned on and connected to the mentioned computer. |

### Configure Printers

By clicking the 'Configure Printers' button you can view all configured printers for this tenancy and configure new printers. You can configure printers for certain Customers, Model (entity in CartonCloud), User, Type and Print Format. See [Configuring Multiple Printers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Configuring-Multiple-Printers) and [Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Printing-from-CartonCloud) for more information.

### Troubleshooting printing issues

From the Remote Print Jobs screen you can diagnose and troubleshoot printing issues. Please see [Troubleshooting Printing](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Troubleshooting-Printing) for troubleshooting steps.

<a id="print-warehouse-location-labels"></a>
## Print Warehouse Location Labels

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/print-warehouse-location-labels_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to print your warehouse location labels
- Suggested stationary
- Printing warehouse locations using Avery templates
- Printing warehouse locations for custom label sizes

### Purpose

To print out your Warehouse Location labels.
**Please note, that this setup is restricted to Warehouse Locations that are 14 characters or less.**

### How to print your warehouse location labels

If you have a large number of labels to print, we suggest following [Printing Warehouse Location Labels using Avery Templates.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Printing-Warehouse-Location-Labels-using-Avery-Templates)

When you print labels from CartonCloud, they will automatically fit on A4 size paper. Because of this, you can use PPS label paper to easily mass-produce precut labels which can then be peeled off and directly applied to a location. See the bottom of the page for the suggested stationery.

- Navigate to the Warehouse Locations page, Warehouse > Warehouse Locations .
- Then select the Warehouse Locations you would like to print on the page. To select the entire page (like in the animation below), select the top warehouse location, then while holding the SHIFT key select the bottom location. You can also use the CTRL key to select or unselect a single location if required.
- Once all desired locations are selected, use the Print Locations Labels button to print to your A4 printer. Ensure it is loaded with sticker sheets if you are using them before printing. As large quantities of label paper can be expensive, we highly recommend printing a single test sheet first and checking the paper is loaded in the printer with adhesive on the correct side.
- You will now need to repeat this process for each page of locations in CartonCloud until all Warehouse Locations are printed.

### Suggested stationary

For PPS labels in Australia: PPS78165 8x labels per A4 sheet at 99.1mm x 67.7mm size. Available from [Officeworks](https://www.officeworks.com.au/shop/officeworks/p/pps-mailing-labels-100-sheets-8-per-page-pps78165?searchTerm=PPS78165)

For PPS labels in New Zealand: Available from [Warehouse Stationery](https://www.warehousestationery.co.nz/product/W2451150.html#q=Mailing+labels&sz=24&start=1)

For PPS labels in Canada: 8.5 x 11" paper with a label size of 4" x 2" from [Staples](https://www.staples.ca/products/12243-en-avery-trueblock-laserinkjet-shipping-labels-4-x-2-white-1000-pack-5163)

### Printing warehouse locations using Avery templates

For an easy and efficient way of printing your warehouse location labels using Avery Templates please refer to [Printing Warehouse Location Labels using Avery Templates.](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Printing-Warehouse-Location-Labels-using-Avery-Templates)

### Printing warehouse locations for custom label sizes

If you have warehouse location names that are longer than 14 characters (including spaces and hyphens), you can use the following guide to export your Warehouse Locations and print them with custom label sizes.

This method also provides an alternative to printing labels in bulk rather than page by page through the web app.

For a wider label, try Product Code [AV959007](https://www.officeworks.com.au/shop/officeworks/p/avery-6up-laser-shipping-labels-100-sheets-av959007#specifications) (the software code for the Mail Merge is L7166)

**If you haven't already, you will need to download a barcode font for [Windows](https://fonts2u.com/free-3-of-9-regular.font%C2%A0or%C2%A0http://www.barcodelink.net/barcode-font.php)**

**Step 1: Printing Warehouse Locations**

To create the mail merge, you will need to begin by exporting your warehouse locations.

To export your Warehouse Locations from the Warehouse Locations Screen, select **More**, then **Export to XLS.**

### Creating Barcode Labels

For all remaining instructions on how to create the barcodes, you will need to follow this [guide](https://www.morovia.com/kb/Tutorial-Creating-barcode-labels-Microsoft-Word-Mail-Merge-10028.html)

Product Code for the wider label above is L7166

<a id="printing-from-cartoncloud"></a>
## Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/printing-from-cartoncloud_

### Table of Contents

- CartonCloud Connect
- Downloading CartonCloud Connect
- How CartonCloud Connect works
- Setup instructions
- Reset password
- Printing

### CartonCloud Connect

CartonCloud Connect is an application that allows you to print directly from within CartonCloud to your printer. Currently, only printers that can handle ZPL format are supported, however, PDF print will be introduced in the future.

### Downloading CartonCloud Connect

The CartonCloud Connect software is available for download from:
Please note that there's no PrintNode Client for iOS.  You can run the PrintNode Client on any computer running Windows, macOS or Linux.  If you want to run it on a tablet, a Windows 10 tablet should be able to do the job.

| Operating   System | Link |
| --- | --- |
| Windows | [https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/windows](https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/windows) |
| Mac | [https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/osx](https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/osx) If using a Mac you will need to download and install a RAW printer driver to run PrintNode (see [Setting up RAW printing for Macs](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/raw-printing-for-osx)). |

### How CartonCloud Connect Works

By installing CartonCloud Connect on to your computer (that is connected to your printer), you will be able to process print jobs sent from CartonCloud. You can initiate a print job from any device connected to CartonCloud and it will print on the specified printer.

![Printing_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Printing_1.avif)

### Setup Instructions

To set up CartonCloud Connect on your computer and enable printing from CartonCloud follow the below steps.

1. Install and connect your printer to the computer.
  - To successfully print from your selected printer the below conditions must be met;
    - The printer must be turned on when processing a printing job.
    - The computer must be connected to the printer (either directly or through the network).
    - The computer must be connected to the internet.
2. Install the CartonCloud Connect application on your computer.
  - Download the software and follow the install instructions using the below links:
    - Windows [https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/windows](https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/windows)
    - [Windows install instructions](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/installation/windows)
    - MacOS / osx [https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/osx](https://app.printnode.com/download/client/cartoncloud/osx)
    - [Mac install instructions](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/installation/osx)
  - Log onto CartonCloud Connect using the email and password supplied to you by CartonCloud Service Desk. This is different from your email/password you use to access CartonCloud itself.
  - Lodge a case with the Service Desk via [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com) if you do not have a password.
3. Enable printing through CartonCloud Connect and select the relevant printer from the **Printers** tab (Tip: search for 'CartonCloud Connect' via the search function built into your PC.

![Printing_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_2.jpeg?width=497&height=355&name=Printing_2.jpeg)

4. Enable the relevant printer within the CartonCloud application (you must have Administrator permissions to complete this step).

- Type in Organisation Settings in the Search for anything bar at the top of the application.
- Select the Features & Options tab within Organisation Settings.
- Click the tick-box Network Zebra Printing Enabled under the Printing Configuration heading.
- Select the relevant printer from the Remote Printer drop-down menu.

![Printing_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_3.jpeg?width=559&height=166&name=Printing_3.jpeg)

### Reset Password

NOTE: Your password for CartonCloud Connect is different from your password for CartonCloud itself.

If you need to reset your password please follow the below steps (you must have Administrator permissions to CartonCloud to complete the below steps).

- Type in Organisation Settings in the Search for anything bar at the top of the application.
- Select the Features & Options tab within Organisation Settings.
- In the Printing Configuration section, click the Reset Password button.
- A screen will be displayed showing the email address and a randomly generated password you need to enter into CartonCloud Connect.

### Printing

Once you have completed the above steps you will be able to print from within the CartonCloud application. You will be able to see a **Print Labels** button from within the relevant Sale Orders, Purchase Orders, and Consignments.

If you need a custom label format, please use CartonCloud Help and lodge a case with our support team to discuss your requirements.

**Consignments**

![Printing_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_4.jpeg?width=670&height=132&name=Printing_4.jpeg)

![Printing_5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_5.jpeg?width=449&height=359&name=Printing_5.jpeg)

**Purchase Orders**
![Printing_6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_6.jpeg?width=670&height=132&name=Printing_6.jpeg)
**Sale Orders**
![Printing_7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Printing_7.jpeg?width=670&height=160&name=Printing_7.jpeg)

<a id="troubleshooting-printing"></a>
## Troubleshooting Printing

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/troubleshooting-printing_

### Table of Contents

- Resolving printing issues
- Check 1
- Check 2
- Check 3
- Check 4
- Check 5
- Other possible issues

### Resolving printing issues

If you are experiencing printing issues, there are four different applications you can utilise to identify and resolve the issue. These applications include; the CartonCloud Connect application, PrintNode, CartonCloud, and the device you are using (your computer and printer).

PrintNode is a hosted printing service that runs CartonCloud Connect and enables remote printing from within CartonCloud (refer to the diagram at the bottom of the article for more detailed information). Accessing the PrintNode website whilst troubleshooting is extremely helpful as it stores information relating to all your devices connected to CartonCloud Connect.

Follow the below checks to identify and resolve the printing issue.

### Check 1

The printer is turned on and that your computer shows the printer is connected.

### Check 2

The correct computer and printer are connected to CartonCloud Connect.  You can check this from within CartonCloud or the CartonCloud Connect application.

**CartonCloud Application**

- Navigate to the **Print Log (More > Print Log).**
- From the Print Log screen you will be able to see the printer and computer being utilised by CartonCloud to print the jobs. You will also be able to see if the printer and computer are connected.

![Troubleshooting Printing_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_1.jpeg?width=670&height=99&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_1.jpeg)

**Printer:**

- Offline : this means the printer is not online and will not be able to print. You will need to check the printer is connected to your computer and is turned on.
- Online : this means the printer is online, connected to your computer and should be working as expected. If it is still not printing when it reads as online there must be another issue, please read the other checks.

**Computer:**

- Offline : the computer is not connected to CartonCloud Connect, you will need to connect it in order to be able to print. Please see Printing from CartonCloud (Printer Setup) for more information.
- Connected : the computer is connected to CartonCloud Connect and should be working as expected. If it is still not printing when it reads as Connected there must be another issue, please read the other checks.
- Navigate to the CartonCloud Connect application (see step 3 in setup instructions).
- Under **Account**, check the name of the computer you are using.

![Troubleshooting Printing_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_2.jpeg?width=427&height=287&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_2.jpeg)

- In **Printers,** the name of the connected printer.

![Troubleshooting Printing_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_3.jpeg?width=448&height=292&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_3.jpeg)

- Check: computer and printer on CartonCloud Connect are the same as the CartonCloud application.
- You can confirm that the correct printer is selected by comparing the name in the **Print Log**(within the CartonCloud application) to the printer in **CartonCloud Connect**.

Logging into PrintNode directly will also give you further information when troubleshooting printing issues.

- Navigate to PrintNode website - [https://app.printnode.com/app/login](https://app.printnode.com/app/login). Use the same login details you use to access CartonCloud Connect.
- View**Devices.**
- A list of the connected devices will be displayed. Make the computer and printer you are attempting to use are connected.
- Use this view to resolve the connection and duplicate printing issues (where more than one device has a session of CartonCloud connect running).

![Troubleshooting Printing_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_4.jpeg?width=476&height=273&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_4.jpeg)

- In**Print Something**you canview the Print History and ensure the correct devices are being utilised.

![Troubleshooting Printing_5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_5.jpeg?width=476&height=327&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_5.jpeg)

### Check 3

Check that your network/server is stable and you are connected to it.

**CartonCloud Connect**

- Select L**ogs** From the menu options in the CartonCloud Connect application.
- Confirm connection for your printer and device.
- If you see that there has been a disconnection:
  - Check the printer and computer are connected to the same network.
  - Check with your IT team if there have been any recent server updates or internal network changes that would have caused the disconnection.

![Troubleshooting Printing_6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_6.jpeg?width=518&height=219&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_6.jpeg)

![Troubleshooting Printing_7](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_7.jpeg?width=522&height=164&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_7.jpeg)

### Check 4

Check the error messages in CartonCloud or PrintNode.

**CartonCloud**

- Navigate to More>Print Log.
- Check the State column against the relevant print job to check it has been completed or not.

![Troubleshooting Printing_8](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_8.jpeg?width=670&height=99&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_8.jpeg)

- You can also check the Title, Entity and Warehouse to better understand what jobs are not printing and troubleshoot from there.

**PrintNode**

- In the PrintNode website, view **Print Something**.
- Check the print history for errors.
- If there is an error you will see it in the **State** column.
- Using the arrow next to the created date to expand the print job further details will be shown detailing the error.

![Troubleshooting Printing_9](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_9.jpeg?width=529&height=333&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_9.jpeg)

**Error examples:**
"[WinError13StartDocPrinter()]The data is invalid" - This is a Windows error and restarting the Print Spooler Windows Service or restarting the computer should be able to fix the issue.

"[WinError 1801 OpenPrinter()] The printer name is invalid." - This is a Windows error and likely relating to the Firewall / Anti Virus settings on your computer or an issue with the printer drivers that have been installed.

### Check 5

If using a Mac, check that a RAW printer driver is being used to run PrintNode (see [Setting up RAW printing for Macs](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/raw-printing-for-osx)).

**Test Print Job**

During troubleshooting, it can be useful to test print jobs through PrintNode.

- Select **Print Something**within PrintNode.

![Troubleshooting Printing_10](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_10.jpeg?width=467&height=163&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_10.jpeg)

- From the Source drop-down source menu, select either Upload a file (if you have a file you wish to test) or PrintNode Test Page (to use one of the supplied test print pages).
- Select the printer.
- Or use the drag and drop option and place the file in the Upload File field.

**Label Size Issues**

In some cases, Zebra printers may print CartonCloud labels in a different size, to avoid this, the printer should be installed as a Raw printer.

RAW printing is sending a string of commands to a printer directly in its native language. Many printers that are popular with PrintNode users support this. RAW printing bypasses the printer's drivers, making it very fast and reliable. It is perfect for printing receipts, barcodes, and text-based labels.

**Install your RAW printer on the same computer that is running the CartonCloud Connect application**

Windows Instructions: [https://qz.io/wiki/setting-up-a-raw-printer-in-windows](https://qz.io/wiki/setting-up-a-raw-printer-in-windows)

Mac OSX Instructions: [https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/raw-printing-for-osx](https://www.printnode.com/en/docs/raw-printing-for-osx)

**Printing Workflow**

![Troubleshooting Printing_11](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Troubleshooting%20Printing_11.jpeg?width=670&height=223&name=Troubleshooting%20Printing_11.jpeg)

### Other possible issues

**It's printing more than 1 copy of labels**

This can happen if CartonCloud Connect is running multiple times on the one machine or is installed on multiple machines.

The most common cause is the application is running underneath multiple users simultaneously on one machine. For example, it's running on a server in the background under the Administrator login, then a user logs in and re-runs the application under their own account. Now, the application is running twice on the system and therefore will collect and print the labels within each open application.

To resolve, close the program under one or more of the users until the issue disappears.

This can also occur if you are running CartonCloud Connect on a server and it is not running as a Windows Service (runs for every user).

In this case, uninstall the CartonCloud Connect app off the server entirely and reinstall it as a Windows Service (this will stop the system from running multiple times).

**Labels Misaligned**

Almost always this is due to local printer settings refer to the guide that came with your printer "re-calibrate your printer"

**How do I use multiple printers?**

CartonCloud enables you to use multiple Zebra printers and define when printers are used (by user or process or a combination of both) Refer [Configuring Multiple printers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Configuring+Multiple+printers)

**Can I change my Labels?**

At present only PDF labels can be customised. Refer [Document Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Document+Templates); this means that for custom labels that you have designed yourself you must download then print (direct Zebra printing will be coming in the future)

For additional fields such as Batch Numbers, refer to the above and [Document Template Placeholders](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/V2+Document+Template+Placeholders)

---

# Account Management > Reporting

<a id="api-client-usage-report"></a>
## API Client Usage Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/api-client-usage-report_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to run the API Client Report

### Purpose

The API Clients Report will show the last four weeks of API Client activity. It will detail the number of API calls made per week per API Client. In addition, it will highlight what Customers and Warehouses are associated with each API Client.

An API call is when the API Client either requests or sends information to CartonCloud.

**Please see the [API Clients page](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/API-Clients) for information on what an API Client is and how to create one.**

### How to Run the API Client Report

- Navigate to the API Client Usage Report, Reports>API Client Usage Report.
- Click the green Show Report button.

![api-client-usage-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-client-usage-report-0.png?width=670&height=147&name=api-client-usage-report-0.png)

- The report will then be displayed on the page.
- You will be able to see the number of API Clients and the total number of calls made each week for all API Clients.

![api-client-usage-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/api-client-usage-report-1.png?width=670&height=252&name=api-client-usage-report-1.png)

<a id="automation-report"></a>
## Automation Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/automation-report_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Dashboard quickview
- Manual vs automated
- Automation report explained
- How to improve automation levels

### Purpose

The Automation Report is a powerful tool to allow you easily check which of your Customer's are entering their orders manually or having your staff enter their orders manually.

### Dashboard Quickview

You can see a quick breakdown of the report from the Dashboard screen. If you don't see this widget then simply [enable it](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Dashboard) through the dashboard.

![automation-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/automation-report-0.png?width=467&height=256&name=automation-report-0.png)

### Manual vs Automated

The following table explains the various data-entry types and whether they are considered manual or automated.

| **Automated / Manual** | **Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Manual | Manual (Admin) | Jobs manually keyed in by your staff. |
| Manual | Manual (Customer) | Jobs manually keyed in by your customers. (user logged in as "Customer") |
| Automated | Email | Jobs imported via email. |
| Automated | FTP | Jobs imported via FTP. |
| Automated | Web Upload | Jobs imported through a file via Web Upload (includes those uploaded by customers) |
| Automated | API | Jobs imported through the [CartonCloud API](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/) |
| Automated | From Sale Order | Consignments created automatically from a Sale Order |

### Automation Report Explained

Clicking on any of the bars will open the Automation Report.

The report provides you with a visualisation of how jobs were created last week, categorising them into the way in which the data was entered.

![automation-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/automation-report-1.png?width=433&height=556&name=automation-report-1.png)

**Week on week comparison**

The report also includes a week by week comparison on the level of automation within your operation and the break down of where data is coming from into your system. This provides further insight on the data entry efficiency of your operation over a period of time going back up to a month.

![automation-report-2-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/automation-report-2-1.png?width=670&height=170&name=automation-report-2-1.png)
**Which customers are costing the most time**

To assist you in knowing where to focus your automation efforts, the report lists **up to 10** of your most manual customers.
Note: You can access more details across all customers through [CartonCloud BI](https://www.cartoncloud.com/bi-dashboard)

![automation-report-3-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/automation-report-3-1.png?width=670&height=133&name=automation-report-3-1.png)

### How to improve automation levels

We're here to help you get data entry automated. So simply [get in contact with our integrations team](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and we can work with you to get things automated.

---

<a id="bulk-charges-report"></a>
## Bulk Charges Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bulk-charges-report_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to run the report
- Columns of the report
- Example report

### Purpose

The Bulk Charges Report allows Administrator users (who can view charging information) to create and export reports containing charging data for a specified date range, entity (Sale Order, Purchase Order, Storage Period and/or Consignment) and for selected customers. The Bulk Charges Report is designed to allow for more granular analysis of charges, facilitating better financial oversight and decision making. In addition, the report can be run via the API. See [here](https://api-docs.cartoncloud.com/#reports) for more information.

### How to run the report

*Note: data from all warehouses will be included in the export and the report limit is 20,000 rows.*

*Note: only charges that have been generated against an order will show on the report. If the charges against an order haven't yet been generated they will not appear on the report.*

- Click **Reports** >**Bulk Export Charges**.
- Select a **Date Filter**. Select to filter the report by either the **Created Date**,**Invoice Date** or **Activity Date** of the related entity to the charge.
  - **Created Date**: Works off the Sale Order/Purchase Order/Consignment/Storage Period created date.
  - **Invoice Date**: Works off the invoice start/end dates and will also include invoices that overlap the supplied date range.
  - **Activity Date:** Works off the date an activity took place, which includes:
    - Sale Order: The date the order was packed.
    - Consignments: The date the Consignment was delivered.
    - Purchase Order: The date the Purchase Order was allocated.
    - Run Sheet: The delivery date for the Run Sheet.
    - Manifests: The date the Manifest was added.
- Select a **From** and **To** date. This date and time is respective to your local time zone.
- Select the **Customers** you wish to include in the Report (only active customers will be visible here) or leave blank to export all.
- Select the **Applies to** you wish to include in the report or leave blank to export all. You can choose Consignment, Manifest, Sale Order, Purchase Order, Storage Period or Run Sheet.
- Click **Export Excel**.

*![bulk-charges-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-charges-report-0.png?width=670&height=227&name=bulk-charges-report-0.png)*

- Download the report from the notification bar in the top right corner.

Note: Any charges linked to a **Voided Invoice** will not be included in the report.

### Columns of the report

| **Column heading** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Id | Id of the charge |
| UUID | UUID of the charge |
| Created Date | Date the related entity was created |
| Customer | The Customer the charge relates to |
| Parent Entity | The related entity, for example, Sale Order |
| Parent Reference | The reference for the related entity |
| Parent Id | Id of the related entity |
| Parent UUID | UUID of the related entity |
| Invoice Id | Invoice Id of the invoice related to the charge |
| Invoice Internal Reference | The CartonCloud internal invoice reference, e.g W.E 11/02/25 (CartonCloud: 4775) |
| Invoice External Reference | The CartonCloud external invoice reference, e.g INV-4372 |
| Invoice Start Date | Invoice start date of the related invoice to the charge |
| Invoice End Date | Invoice end date of the related invoice to the charge |
| Type | The type of charge |
| Automatic | If the charge is applied automatically |
| Fee Category | Fee category of the charge |
| Account | The account the charge sits on in terms of the invoice |
| Description | Description of the charge |
| Qty | The number of times the Ad-Hoc Charge or Item Charge is applied to the related order.  The number of pallets being charges for per pallet qty storage charges |
| Charge | The charge amount |
| Warehouse Name | What Warehouse the charge relates to |
| Activity Date | If the report is run by Activity Date, the date the activity occurred |
| Fuel Levy Amount | The total fuel levy charge applied to the line item. This value represents the calculated fuel surcharge included in the charge. |
| Fuel % | The percentage rate used to calculate the fuel levy for the charge |

### Example report

![bulk-charges-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-charges-report-1.png?width=670&height=230&name=bulk-charges-report-1.png)

<a id="business"></a>
## Business Intelligence Tool

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/business_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Benefits
- Considerations
- Explanation of each Dashboard and data
- How to apply and change filters on a Dashboard
- How to export Visuals
- BI tool webinar ​​​​​​​

**Please note this is a [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) only feature. For more information on [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/WMS-Premium) and to upgrade your account please reach out to our Service Desk team [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).**

### Purpose

The Business Intelligence (BI) Tool is an analysis tool that provides you with historical information that will provide you with valuable insights into your Operation.

To gain access to the BI Tool please [contact us](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket).

### Benefits

- Greater visibility - the BI dashboard enables users to analyse data to make better decisions. Whether it's preparing for rate changes, reviewing which warehouse pickers are the most efficient, or identifying which customers require the most data entry. All of this is available at the click of a button.
- Improve relationships - Strengthen your customer relationships by providing your clients with insights into their own business. CartonCloud BI allows you to evaluate data on a per-customer level so you can notify your clients of trends your seeing in their business. Use these insights to position yourself as a premium provider and make your customer relationships sticky.
- Navigate Change - As the saying goes, "Change is the only constant in business". Shifts in volumes, delivery locations, customer revenue, fast moving products, and staff efficiency all occur over time. CartonCloud BI allows you to spot these trends early,  enabling you to better position your business sooner, and converting change from a hassle into an opportunity.

### Considerations

- There a number of Dashboards available and each Dashboard contains a large number of graphs, tables, data highlights and summaries.
- The type of graphs and how they are formatted is not customisable, however, there is a large variety of different graphs, tables and summaries that allow you to easily analyse data and make decisions. In addition, you can apply different filters to the existing graphs and data.
- Filters can be applied to each Dashboard at either the Dashboard or individual visual level. For example, you may filter by a certain Customer or change the date range displayed.
- The available Dashboards include:
  - Summary
  - Drivers (TMS only)
  - Consignments (TMS only)
  - Sale Orders (WMS only)
  - SO Products (WMS only)
  - Purchase Orders (WMS only)

### Explanation of each Dashboard and the Visuals

For definitions of each Visual per Dashboard see [BI Dashboards Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/BI-Dashboards-Explained)

### How to apply and change filters on a Dashboard

- Hover your mouse over the data/graph on the Dashboard you wish to apply a filter for and select the Filter icon in the top right corner.

![business-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-0.png?width=670&height=295&name=business-0.png)

- Select View Dashboard filters .

![business-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-1.png?width=670&height=335&name=business-1.png)

- If you wish to add a new filter, click Add Filter .

![business-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-2.png?width=458&height=364&name=business-2.png)

- Select the field you wish to filter by.
- Click the filter you just selected.
- Select if you wish to apply the filter at the individual or Dashboard level.

![business-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-3.png?width=466&height=369&name=business-3.png)

- Select the filter type, it is suggested you use Filter list (filter the list of values) or Custom Filter (allows you to use conditions to filter by).
- Select the filter condition.
- Enter or select the values to filter by.

![business-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-4.png?width=148&height=397&name=business-4.png)

- Click Apply .

### How to export Visuals

To export a visual you will need to:

- Hover over the Visual you wish to export.
- Select the three-dot icon, Menu options in the top right corner and then Export to CSV.

![business-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/business-5.png?width=670&height=282&name=business-5.png)

### BI Tool Webinar

We held a Webinar back in March which provided an overview of the functionality within the BI tool.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/8g-QOXZT2I4

<a id="consignment-invoice-report"></a>
## Consignment Invoice Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-invoice-report_

To navigate to the Consignment Invoice Report select **Reports** in the main menu followed by**Consignment Invoice Report** in the drop-down menu.

If Consignment Invoices are being used for either [Superimposed Proof Of Delivery](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Superimposed+Proof+Of+Delivery) or [Driver Scan Allocation](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Driver+Scan+Allocation) with the [QR Code Overlay for Invoices](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/QR+Code+Overlay+for+Invoices), the Consignment Invoice Report can be used to quickly check which Consignments do or don't have Invoices attached to them.

Select the date you want the report to run for, configure the other options such as displaying Future Dated Consignments and whether or not to show delivered consignments and click "Search".
The report will then show you which Consignments do or don't have Invoices uploaded, and you can click on the numbers to go immediately to those jobs.

![consignment-invoice-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-invoice-report-0.png?width=670&height=249&name=consignment-invoice-report-0.png)
