<a id="consignment-report"></a>
## Consignment Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-report_

### Table of Contents

- How to navigate to the consignment report
- Report overview
- Report columns
- Consignment notification

### How to navigate to the consignment report

To navigate to the Consignment Report page:

- Select **Reports**>**Consignment Report**in the drop-down menu.

This feature is available for both Warehouse Management System (WMS) and Transport Management System (TMS) customers.

### Report overview

The Consignment Report is used to generate custom reports on consignment activity, predominantly on recently delivered consignments.  The report is viewable either in the web browser by clicking the **Show Report**button or by exporting the report into a CSV file by using the **Export Excel** button. It can also be sent as part of a daily consignment report notification.

The report is customisable and can be saved as a "Report Template" for later use.

Report Filters

![consignment-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-0.png?width=533&height=109&name=consignment-report-0.png)

1. **Customer (Admin Only)**: Either run the report over all your customers or just for a specific customer.

2.**Order By**: The order in which the report is sorted.

3.**Date Filter**: In combination with **4. From** and **5. To** this is used to filter the report to a specific date range (e.g. all consignments delivered today).

6. **Delivery Status**: Current status of the consignment (e.g. Awaiting Pickup, In Transit (Pickup → Warehouse), Delivered, Delivered (Warehouse Fulfilment). To view the available statuses, please see [Consignment Types](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-types).

### Report Columns

Below are a list and description of all the fields that can be used in this report. For any that are custom fields (*".. Custom Fields"*), these will show all available custom fields in the report. Each custom field will have a separate header and appear in the order they were set up.

**Transport Fields**

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Customer ID | The id of the customer |
| Customer Name | The name of the customer |
| Consignment Reference | The reference of the consignment |
| Date Delivered | The date the consignment was delivered |
| Consignment Date Modified | The date the consignment was last modified |
| Consignment ID | The id of the consignment |
| Consignment Income | The income of the consignment. Note, with grouped consignments, parent consignments will display the income data aggregated from the associated child consignments. Child consignments will reference the parent consignment, however, will not show income data and will appear as $0. |
| Consignment Expense | The expense of the consignment |
| Consignment Date Added | The date the consignment was added |
| Consignment Invoice ID | The id of the consignment invoice |
| Group Consignment ID | The id of the consignment's group. |
| Group Consignment | Yes if the consignment is part of a group, else No. |
| Cash On Delivery | How much cash on delivery for the consignment. |
| Consignment Value | The value of the consignment |
| Consignment Delivery Status | The current delivery status of the consignment e.g. Awaiting Pickup |
| Consignment Custom Fields | All enabled consignment custom fields. |
| Consignment Data Custom Fields | All enabled consignment data custom fields. |
| Delivery Run Date | The delivery date of the delivery run. |
| Delivery Run | The name of the delivery run. |
| Pickup Company Name | The company name of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Street Address | The street address of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Suburb | The suburb of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup City | The city of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Postcode | The postcode of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup State | The state of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Delivery Address ID | The id of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Address | The full address of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Company Name | The company name of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Street Address | The street address of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Suburb | The suburb of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery City | The city of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Postcode | The postcode of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery State | The state of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery ID | The delivery id of the consignment |
| Manifest ID | The manifest id of the consignment |
| Driver Name | The name of the driver for the consignment |
| Vehicle Name | The name of the vehicle for the consignment |
| Mobile App Custom Fields | The Mobile App Custom Fields. See: [Custom Fields within the App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/POD+Fields+Customisation) |

**Consignment Item Fields**

You can choose to display the Consignment Item fields of the Consignment. If you do this, each Consignment Item associated with the Consignment will show as an individual line.

Considerations when using Consignment Item fields

- If the Consignment has a Sale Order associated with it, the Sale Order fields will show as a new line below the Consignment Item lines (an astricts * will sign that the Consignment has a Sale Order associated with it).
- If using the Consignment Item Custom Fields, you can not select individual Custom Fields; therefore, all Custom Fields will be displayed.
- When using Consignment Item Fields, load times for the report may increase.
- If using Consignment Custom Fields, note that this field relates to the total Consignment, so it will not show line item details.

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Consignment Item Code | The code of the Consignment Item's Transport Product e.g CAR for Carton |
| Consignment Item Description | The description of the Consignment Item's Transport Products e.g Carton |
| Consignment Item Qty | The quantity of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Pallets | The number of pallets of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Spaces | The number of spaces of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Cubic | The cubic of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Weight | The weight of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Length | The length of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Width | The width of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Height | The height of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Custom Fields | The Consignment Item Custom Fields. Note you can not select individual Custom Fields; therefore, all Custom Fields will show. They will be displayed in the same order in the Consignment Item UI. |

**Warehouse Fields**

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Sale Order Reference | The reference on the sale order |
| Sale Order Date added | The date the sale order was added |
| Sale Order ID | The id of the sale order |
| Sale Order Delivery Status | The current delivery status of the sale order e.g. Awaiting Pick and Pack |
| Order Qty | The original number of units of a product requested for this sale order |
| Ship Qty | The number of units of a product that were dispatched with this consignment |
| Product Code | The code of the product |
| Product Name | The name of the product |
| Product Type | The type of product |
| Unit of Measure | The unit of measure used by the product |
| Expiry date | The expiry date of the product |
| Pop Custom Fields | The purchase order product custom fields (e.g. Batch Number) |

### Consignment Notification

It is possible to automatically send daily Consignment Reports to Customers through their notification settings.

To do this:

- Select **Contacts**>**Customers**.
- Select the Customer whom you wish to set up notifications for.

![consignment-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-1.png?width=670&height=140&name=consignment-report-1.png)

- Click Edit .

![consignment-report-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-2.png?width=670&height=156&name=consignment-report-2.png)

- Select the Email tab and then the Notifications tab. Confirm that **Send Daily Consignment Report Email** is enabled.

![consignment-report-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-3.png?width=670&height=154&name=consignment-report-3.png)

![consignment-report-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-4.png?width=670&height=41&name=consignment-report-4.png)

- Under the Email tab and then under the Addresses sub-tab, either edit an existing notification or add a new email address.

![consignment-report-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-5.png?width=670&height=143&name=consignment-report-5.png)

- Tick the **Consignment Notification**box and add the desired templates. These templates will be part of the Consignment Notification emails, which are sent out daily.

![consignment-report-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-6.png?width=670&height=102&name=consignment-report-6.png)
The Report Templates will be sent as an attachment with the name of the attachment used as the Report Template name (so name them wisely!) The attachments are sent as CSV files and contain exactly the same format/columns/data as can be extracted by exporting the report through the web app. One crucial difference is that it does not use both filters, rather it uses whichever filter you selected in the Run Email Notification Over. The options are:

1. **Last Day**: This uses the Report Template's saved *Date Filter and Delivery Status*and runs the report over the last day. For example, if date filter was set to date delivered and the delivery status was all and the date was the 18th then the email sent would contain an attachment with all consignments delivered on the 18th.
2. **Last 3 Months**: This uses the Report Template's saved *Delivery Status* and behaves exactly the same as the first option except it runs the report over the past three months.

Report Templates will not be sent if no consignments match the criteria defined in the template. This is to prevent users from being spammed daily with empty reports. If multiple attachments are supposed to be part of the email and only one has any consignments, just one attachment will be sent.

---

<a id="consignment-report-customer"></a>
## Consignment Report (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/consignment-report-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Report overview
- Report template
- Report columns
- Consignment item fields
- Warehouse fields

### Report overview

The Consignment Report is a valuable report that provides insight into Consignment activity. It offers the ability to filter and display Consignments based on specific criteria, such as the order status. In addition, the Consignment Report allows for the creation of templates, which are pre-configured formats that can be applied when creating your report.

### How to create a Consignment Report

- Navigate to the Consignment Report, Reports > Consignment Report .
- Select how you wish to order the report from the Order By drop down
  - Consignment Reference
  - Date Added
  - Date Modified
  - Delivered Date
  - Delivery Run Date
- Select how you wish the report to be filtered from the Date Filter drop down
  - Date Added
  - Date Delivered
  - Date Modified
  - Delivery Run Date
  - Delivery Run Date or Date Delivered
- Select the Delivery Status you wish to include in the report from the drop down
- You can then choose what fields you wish to be included in the report. The below table defines each field.
- Click Show Report (show on the web page) or Export Excel (to export the report in an excel format).

### Report Template

See [Creating Report Templates](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+Report+Templates) for more information on how to create and use Report Templates.

For this report, the Report Template will also capture the Delivery Status and the Date Filter. When you switch between Report Templates these will update automatically. These are useful to set up as they greatly affect what the report displays.

![consignment-report-customer-0-png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/consignment-report-customer-0-png.png?width=538&height=65&name=consignment-report-customer-0-png.png)

### Report Columns

Below are a list and description of all the fields that can be used in this report. For any that are custom fields (*".. Custom Fields"*), these will show all available custom fields in the report. Each custom field will have a separate header and appear in the order they were set up.

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Consignment Reference | The reference of the consignment |
| Date Delivered | The date the consignment was delivered |
| Consignment Date Modified | The date the consignment was last modified |
| Consignment ID | The id of the consignment |
| Consignment Income | The income of the consignment |
| Consignment Expense | The expense of the consignment |
| Consignment Date Added | The date the consignment was added |
| Consignment Invoice ID | The id of the consignment invoice |
| Group Consignment ID | The id of the consignments group |
| Group Consignment | Yes if the consignment is part of a group, else No |
| Cash on Delivery | How much cash on delivery for the consignment |
| Consignment Value | The value of the consignment |
| Consignment Delivery Status | The current delivery status of the consignment eg Awaiting Pickup |
| Consignment Custom Fields | All enabled consignment custom fields |
| Consignment Data Custom Fields | All enabled consignment data custom fields |
| Delivery Run Date | The delivery date of the delivery run |
| Delivery Run | The name of the delivery run |
| Pickup Company Name | The company name of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Street Address | The street address of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Suburb | The suburb of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup City | The city of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup Postcode | The postcode of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Pickup State | The state of the consignment's pickup address. |
| Delivery Address ID | The id of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Address | The full address of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Company Name | The company name of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Street Address | The street address of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Suburb | The suburb of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery City | The city of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery Postcode | The postcode of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery State | The state of the consignment's delivery address. |
| Delivery ID | The delivery id of the consignment |
| Manifest ID | The manifest id of the consignment |
| Driver Name | The name of the driver for the consignment |
| Vehicle Name | The name of the vehicle for the consignment |
| Mobile App Custom Fields | The Mobile App Custom Fields. See: [Custom Fields within the App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/POD+Fields+Customisation) |

### Consignment Item Fields

You can choose to display the Consignment Item fields of the Consignment. If you do this, each Consignment Item associated with the Consignment will show as an individual line.

Considerations when using Consignment Item fields

- If the Consignment has a Sale Order associated with it, the Sale Order fields will show as a new line below the Consignment Item lines (an astricts * will sign that the Consignment has a Sale Order associated with it).
- If using the Consignment Item Custom Fields, you can not select individual Custom Fields; therefore, all Custom Fields will be displayed.
- When using Consignment Item Fields, load times for the report may increase.
- If using Consignment Custom Fields, note that this field relates to the total Consignment, so it will not show line item details.

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Consignment Item Code | The code of the Consignment Item's Transport Product e.g CAR for Carton |
| Consignment Item Description | The description of the Consignment Item's Transport Products e.g Carton |
| Consignment Item Qty | The quantity of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Pallets | The number of pallets of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Spaces | The number of spaces of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Cubic | The cubic of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Weight | The weight of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Length | The length of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Width | The width of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Height | The height of the Consignment Item |
| Consignment Item Custom Fields | The Consignment Item Custom Fields. Note you can not select individual Custom Fields; therefore, all Custom Fields will show. They will be displayed in the same order in the Consignment Item UI. |

### Warehouse Fields

| **Field Name** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Sale Order Reference | The reference on the sale order |
| Sale Order Date added | The date the sale order was added |
| Sale Order ID | The id of the sale order |
| Sale Order Delivery Status | The current delivery status of the sale order e.g. Awaiting Pick and Pack |
| Order Qty | The original number of units of a product requested for this sale order |
| Ship Qty | The number of units of a product that were dispatched with this consignment |
| Product Code | The code of the product |
| Product Name | The name of the product |
| Product Type | The type of product |
| Unit of Measure | The unit of measure used by the product |
| Expiry date | The expiry date of the product |
| Pop Custom Fields | The purchase order product custom fields (e.g. Batch Number) |

<a id="creating-report-templates"></a>
## Creating Report Templates

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-report-templates_

### Table of Contents

- Saving templates
- Using templates
- Updating existing templates (admin only)
- Deleting templates (admin only)

### Saving templates

It is possible to create saved customised reports that are used on a regular basis as a

Report Templates

which can then be reused.

To save a set of Report Templates in their current order as a reusable template:

1. Select the set of columns you wish to save as a template and make sure they are in the desired order.
2. Click the blue "Save as a Template" button
3. Enter a name for the template into the popup that appears after clicking the button in step 2
4. (Admin only) You can select the visibility level: 'Visible to all' - All Customers can see it. 'Visible to specified Customers' - Select which customers will see this report. 'Visible internally only' - Only administrators can see it.
5. Click the Save button after providing a template name.
6. The popup will close and the name that you just entered for the template will become the selected value for the "Selected Column Template" dropdown

The template will now be available whenever you return to this page.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-38-15-3157-PM.png?width=589&height=298&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-38-15-3157-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-40-47-5644-PM.png?width=594&height=307&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-40-47-5644-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-43-09-0122-PM.png?width=563&height=136&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-43-09-0122-PM.png)

### Using Templates

You can use any previously saved template by simply clicking on the dropdown next to the text: *"Use Saved Column Template:"* and picking the desired template option. This modifies the columns in the field to be those that were saved as part of the template.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-47-02-1502-PM.png?width=556&height=131&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-47-02-1502-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-48-14-3121-PM.png?width=574&height=136&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-48-14-3121-PM.png)

### Updating existing templates (admin only)

You can update any existing Column Template except for the Default template. The Update Selected Template button will remain disabled until it detects a change to a template that is not the Default template. To update an existing template:

1. Select the existing template you wish to update.
2. Select additional columns and order them as desired or remove existing columns you no longer want to be part of the template.
3. Click the Update Selected Template button. A loading icon will appear while the changes are saved.
4. Once the icon disappears, a success message will appear if the Updated Template was successfully updated. If an error occurred while trying to save the Updated Template, then an error message will be shown.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-52-24-5298-PM.png?width=620&height=132&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-52-24-5298-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-55-14-9324-PM.png?width=637&height=170&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-55-14-9324-PM.png)

### Deleting Templates (Admin only)

You can delete any existing Column Template except for the Default template. The *Delete Selected Template* button will remain disabled until you change to a template that is not the Default Template. To delete an existing template:

1. Select the existing template you wish to delete
2. Click the *Delete Selected Template* button.
3. After clicking the *Delete selected Template* button an alert message will appear at the top of the screen in the centre.
4. Click *OK* in the popup to confirm the delete. A loading icon will then appear after clicking *OK* and will show while the delete is in progress.
5. Once the icon disappears, a success message will appear if the template was successfully deleted. At this time the *Selected Column Template* dropdown will revert back to "*Default*". If an error occurred while trying to delete the template, then an error message will be shown.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-56-55-7538-PM.png?width=1328&height=264&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-56-55-7538-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-58-17-6347-PM.png?width=421&height=134&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-04-58-17-6347-PM.png)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Feb-27-2026-05-00-30-8115-PM.png?width=610&height=181&name=image-png-Feb-27-2026-05-00-30-8115-PM.png)

<a id="customer-stock-report"></a>
## Customer Stock Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-stock-report_

### Table of Contents

- What is the customer stock report
- How to create the customer stock report
- Explanation of in warehouse, free, incoming and allocated
- Customer specific templates

### What is the customer stock report

The Customer Stock Report is used to track the inventory of all Products stores in the given warehouse (that the report is being run on).

You can view the report in the web browser by clicking the **Show Report** button or you can export the report into an XLS file by clicking **Export Excel**.

Various columns can be added to the report for further customisation. The available columns are covered in the section below.

### How to create the customer stock report

- Navigate to Customer Stock Report, Reports > Customer Stock Report .
- Select a specific Customer you wish to run the report for or select All to include all Customers.
- Select the columns you wish to include in the report by typing the column name and selecting from the drop-down. You can click +Add All Columns to include all columns or select the x on a column to remove it from the selection.

![customer-stock-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-report-0.png?width=670&height=202&name=customer-stock-report-0.png)

- The below table covers the columns that can be added to the report. Columns that are not included below are custom fields - the fields you have set up for your Customer. This will include fields such as batch number or serial number.

**The default columns are locked and can not be removed. These columns will not have a x option on the name to remove it.**

| **Column Name** | **Locked** | **Description** | **Available to Customers** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Code | Yes | The code of the Product line | Yes |
| Product Name | Yes | The name of the Product line | Yes |
| Product Status | Yes | The status of the Product line | Yes |
| UOM | Yes | The Unit Of Measure of the Product line | Yes |
| Location | No | The Warehouse Location of the Product line | No |
| In Warehouse | Yes | The amount of stock in the Warehouse of the Product line. This amount is a sum of both Allocated and Free columns | Yes |
| Allocated | No | The amount of stock of the Product line that has been allocated to Sale Orders | Yes |
| Free | Yes | The amount of stock of the Product line that has not been allocated to Sale Orders | Yes |
| Incoming | No | If the Incoming column is part of the report, then the amount of stock on Purchase Orders with a status of Not Yet Received will appear in this column on the Report. | Yes |
| ID | No | The Purchase Order Product (POP) ID. This will show the POPID without the prefix of CCPOPBCP. | Yes |
| Expiry | No | The set Expiry Date of the Product line | Yes |
| Pallet ID | No | If the Product line is stored in a bulk Warehouse Location, then it will show a Pallet Id representing what Pallet it resides on in that Warehouse Location | No |
| Product Group | No | The Product Group of the Product line if any | Yes |
| Product Type | No | The Type of the Product line | Yes |
| Purchase Order Reference | No | The reference of the Purchase Order that the Product line belongs to | Yes |
| Arrival Date | No | The arrival date of the Purchase Order that the Product line belongs to | Yes |
| # Pallets | No | The number of pallets at the given Warehouse Location | Yes |

The Warehouse Stock Report columns can be dragged and dropped in the order desired by simply clicking and dragging a tag to the desired position in the column order. Note that dragging fields to different places in the column order will result in slightly different results being displayed in the report as these options are also used to split the Product lines.

- Alternatively, if you have a saved template you can use that rather than specify the columns you wish to use each time. See Creating Report Templates for more information.
- Select the report options you wish to apply. See below for definitions of the different options.

| **Report Option** | **Description** |
| --- | --- |
| Show Out of Stock Products in Report | If this option is checked then you will both in stock and out of stock products appear in the report. NOTE: If you export the report to excel with this option set then you will get an excel file that has a sheet for In stock products and another sheet for Out of stock products |
| Automatically Scale Units | This option will make all stock counts showing in columns "In Warehouse", "Allocated", "Free", and "Incoming" in their highest possible unit of measure conversion (eg. If the Product line's highest unit of measure is a Pallet, then the counts shown in the report will be in Pallets with this option checked). See below for a way to scale to other UOM levels. |
| Show Stock as at a Historic Date | Checking this option will show a date field to choose which date you want to see stock for |
| Specify Date | This field appears if "Show Stock as at a Historic Date" is checked. You can enter the date you wish to see the historic data for in this field |

- To export the report click Export Excel or Export CSV. It is recommended that you use 'Export CSV' when the file is larger as it will make the download process more efficient. To view the report in the web browser select Show Report .

![customer-stock-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-report-1.png?width=670&height=319&name=customer-stock-report-1.png)

**How the report will appear on the web:**

![customer-stock-report-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-report-2.png?width=670&height=132&name=customer-stock-report-2.png)
**How the report will appear when you download it:**

![customer-stock-report-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-report-3.png?width=670&height=118&name=customer-stock-report-3.png)

### Explanation of In Warehouse, Free, Incoming and Allocated

On the Stock Report, there are four different statuses the inventory can be in.

**In Warehouse:**Is in the warehouse and has not yet been packed in a Sale Order.

**Free**: Is in the warehouse and has not been allocated to a Sale Order yet.

**Incoming:** Stock that is on a Purchase Order but has not yet been received into the warehouse.

**Allocated:**Stock that has been allocated to an order but has not been packed yet.

| Sale Order Status |  |  | Product A Inventory Status |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | In Warehouse | Free | Incoming | Allocated |
| Before Sale Order is raised | 10 | 10 | 0 | 0 |
| Rejected | 10 | 10 | 0 | 0 |
| Draft (Not allocated) | 10 | 10 | 0 | 0 |
| Draft (Stock allocated) | 10 | 5 | 0 | 5 |
| Awaiting Pick and Pack | 10 | 5 | 0 | 5 |
| Packed | 5 | 5 | 0 | 0 |
| Dispatched | 5 | 5 | 0 | 0 |

### Customer specific templates

You can now create and save customer-specific templates, limiting the access to that customer.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/hBdv4uJTlFs

<a id="customer-stock-reports"></a>
## Customer Stock Reports

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/customer-stock-reports_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to generate customer stock reports

### Purpose

From within the View Customer page, you can access Customer-specific Reports.

### How to generate Customer Stock Reports

- Navigate to the Customers page, Contacts > Customers .
- Select the relevant Customer.
- Under Stock Reports select the report you wish to view.
- The below explanations explain what each Report is designed for and how to use it.

![customer-stock-reports-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-0.jpeg?width=670&height=369&name=customer-stock-reports-0.jpeg)

Stock Report (detailed)

This report will show all current stock for the Customer via Warehouse Location or Product. You can export the report to Excel.

You can also edit the stock, add new expiry dates or warehouse locations or adjust the quantities.
![customer-stock-reports-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-1.jpeg?width=670&height=316&name=customer-stock-reports-1.jpeg)
To change the Group By

- Select the Group By drop-down and select the option you wish to apply.
  - **Product - Warehouse Location:**will list the stock by Product and then Warehouse Location.
  - **Product - Expiry date:** will list the stock by Product and then Expiry Date (oldest to newest).
  - **WarehouseLocation - Product:** will list the stock by Warehouse Location and then Product.

To Edit Stocks

Note that you can only edit stocks when you are in the Group By view of Product - Warehouse Location or Product - Expiry Date.

- Select the blue**Edit Stocks** button.
- Make adjustments to the Warehouse Location, Expiry date or quantity.
- Select **Save**.
- Click **Stop Editing Stocks**.

![customer-stock-reports-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-2.jpeg?width=670&height=275&name=customer-stock-reports-2.jpeg)

**Stock Report (Custom)**

For information about the Stock Report (Customer), please see [Customer Stock Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/x/wwGYHw).

**Problem stock report**

The Problem stock report shows all stock for that Customer with a Status other than Ok.
![customer-stock-reports-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-3.jpeg?width=670&height=113&name=customer-stock-reports-3.jpeg)
**Warning stock report**

The Warning stock report will show that customer stock has expired or is within its warning threshold.

![customer-stock-reports-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-4.jpeg?width=670&height=109&name=customer-stock-reports-4.jpeg)

**Product Conversions**

The Product Conversions list all the Customer's Products and the unit of measure conversions.

![customer-stock-reports-5](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-5.jpeg?width=670&height=308&name=customer-stock-reports-5.jpeg)

**Product Expiry/Warning Thresholds**

The Product Expiry/Warning Thresholds list all the Customer's Products and the associated warning and expiry threshold. You can also edit the thresholds either individually for each Product or in bulk.

![customer-stock-reports-6](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/customer-stock-reports-6.jpeg?width=670&height=305&name=customer-stock-reports-6.jpeg)

To edit in bulk:

- Enter the value in the **Set all warning threshold**and **Set all expiry threshold to** the field.
- Click **Set all**.

To edit individually:

- Enter the value within the individual **Warning threshold** and **Expiry threshold**field.
- Click **Save**.

<a id="discrepancy-report"></a>
## Discrepancy Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/discrepancy-report_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Adding a discrepancy report
- Adding consignment errors to the discrepancy report
- Removing consignment errors to the discrepancy report
- Changing the status of a discrepancy report
- Emailing a discrepancy report
- Changing the default email content of a discrepancy report
- Deleting a discrepancy report

### Purpose

Discrepancy Reports are used to track changes and damages in Consignment stock. This is done by using existing Consignment Errors within CartonCloud. To get to the Discrepancy Reports screen:

1. Click on the Reports dropdown on the navigation menu.
2. Click on the **Discrepancy Reports** menu item.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-0-png.png?width=505&height=167&name=discrepancy-report-0-png.png)

3. This will take you to the Discrepancy Reports screen.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-1-png.png?width=1702&height=352&name=discrepancy-report-1-png.png)

### Adding a discrepancy Report

Creating a Discrepancy Report effectively has two steps. The first is to create the actual Discrepancy Report and the second is to add existing Consignment Errors to the Report. To Add a Discrepancy Report:

1. Click the **Add New Report** button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-2-png.png?width=427&height=136&name=discrepancy-report-2-png.png)
    2. This will take you to the Add Discrepancy Report screen.
    3. Choose a Customer for the Report.
    4. Choose a Status for the Report.
    5. Click the **Create Report** button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-3-png.png?width=592&height=175&name=discrepancy-report-3-png.png)

    6. Once the Report is created you will be taken to the View Discrepancy Report screen.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-4-png.png?width=569&height=203&name=discrepancy-report-4-png.png)

### Adding Consignment Errors to the Discrepancy Report

To Add Consignment Errors to the Report:

1. Click on the **Consignment Errors** tab.
2. Click on the **Add Consignment Errors To Report** button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-5-png.png?width=605&height=159&name=discrepancy-report-5-png.png)

3. You will be taken to the Add Consignment Errors To Report screen.

    4. Filter the Consignment errors to select from using the available filters and clicking the **Go!** button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-6-png.png?width=617&height=249&name=discrepancy-report-6-png.png)

5. Clicking the **Go!** button will show a list of Consignment Errors for the Customer that you selected when you first created the Discrepancy Report, filtered by whatever options you selected in the filters.

6. Select the Consignment Errors you want to add to the Report by clicking the checkbox.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-7-png.png?width=1075&height=761&name=discrepancy-report-7-png.png)

7. Click the **Add Consignment Errors To Report** button to add the selected Consignment Errors to the Report.

    8. This will take you back to the Consignment Errors tab on the Discrepancy Report view screen where you will see the selected Consignment Errors appear in the list.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-8-png.png?width=606&height=246&name=discrepancy-report-8-png.png)

### Removing Consignment Errors from Discrepancy Report

To Remove Consignment Errors from a Discrepancy Report:

1. Select the Consignment Errors you want to remove from the Report.
2. Click the **Remove Selected Errors** button.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-9-png.png?width=627&height=228&name=discrepancy-report-9-png.png)
   3. A confirmation will appear after clicking the **Remove Selected Errors** button. Click OK in the confirmation.

### Changing the Status of a Discrepancy Report

To change the status of a Discrepancy Report:![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-10-png.png?width=1163&height=343&name=discrepancy-report-10-png.png)

1. Click on the **Change Status** button which will show a list of available statuses that the Report can be changed to.
2. Click on the Status that you want to change the report to and this will update the Report to have that Status.

### Emailing a Discrepancy Report

To Email a Discrepancy Report

1. Click on the **Send Email** button and a popup will appear containing the formatted Default Email Content as well as the email addresses the Discrepancy Report will be sent to.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-11-png.png?width=457&height=469&name=discrepancy-report-11-png.png)
2. Change the content or email addresses of the email if required. The emails come from the Customer settings emails area. See this guide for how they work - [Emails and Notifications - Configuration of Parsers](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Emails+and+Notifications+-+Configuration+of+Parsers). The content comes from the **Default Discrepancy Report Email Text** in the Organisation Settings. See the **Changing the Default Email Content of a Discrepancy Report** section of this article for more information.

3. Click the **Send** button.

### Changing the Default Email Content of a Discrepancy Report

You can change the default content that appears when sending the Discrepancy Report email by editing the text in the Organisation Settings. To get to the Organisation Settings follow this guide - [Organisation Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/CKB/Organisation+Settings).

Once in the Organisation Settings navigate to the Email tab then scroll down until you reach the Default Discrepancy Report Email Text option.
![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-12-png.png?width=560&height=155&name=discrepancy-report-12-png.png)

To edit the Default Content, type the text you want to appear when sending emails into the editor. You should always make sure that the **{report_content}** field is in the content as this gets replaced with the Consignment Errors that are part of the Discrepancy Report. To save your changes click the **Save** button at the bottom of the screen.
![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-13-png.png?width=605&height=274&name=discrepancy-report-13-png.png)

### Deleting a Discrepancy Report

To Delete a Discrepancy Report:

1. Click on the **Delete** button when viewing the Discrepancy Report.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/discrepancy-report-14-png.png?width=1177&height=326&name=discrepancy-report-14-png.png)

    2. After clicking on the Delete button a confirmation message will appear.
    3. Click on OK to Delete the Report. Once the Report is deleted you will be redirected back to the Discrepancy Reports listing page.

<a id="problem-stock-report-customer"></a>
## Problem Stock Report (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/problem-stock-report-customer_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Problem Stock Report
- How to run a Problem Stock Report

### What is a Problem Stock Report

The Problem Stock Report will generate a list of any stock in the warehouse which has a status other than OK. CartonCloud Administrators can create their own product statuses to easily identify the status of stock. However, by default the included product stases are:

- OK
- Damaged
- Damaged by Carrier
- Lost
- Missing
- Quarantine
- Received Damaged

### How to run a Problem Stock Report

- Select Reports > Problem Stock Report.
- Automatically a list of stock that is in a product status other than OK will show on the screen.
- In the example report below we can see that there are 50 units of Chocolate Biscuit in a Warehouse location which currently have the status set to "Quarantine". There is also 200 Units of Vanilla Extract with the status "Missing" and a further 200 units of Vanilla Extract with the status "Damaged".

![problem-stock-report-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/problem-stock-report-customer-0.png?width=670&height=290&name=problem-stock-report-customer-0.png)

## Purchase Order Report (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-order-report-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Accessing the purchase order report

### Purpose

The Purchase Order Report provides a list of all Purchase Orders and their related data, including custom fields for a specified date range.

### Accessing the purchase order report

- Navigate to the Purchase Order Report, Reports > Purchase Order Report .
- Select if you wish to order the report by Date Added or Arrival Date .
  - Date Added : the date the order was added into CartonCloud
  - Arrival Date : the date it arrived to the warehouse
- Select the Purchase Order History Status you wish to show on the report.
  - All (Verified, Allocated)
  - Verified: Purchase Orders which have arrived but has not yet been allocated to warehouse location.
  - Allocated : Purchase Orders that have arrived and been located to a warehouse location.
- Select the From and To date.
- Click Show Report (will show on the web page) or Export Exce l (will download into an excel format and you will be notified when it is ready via the bell icon in the top right of the screen)

![Purchase Report Customer_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Purchase%20Report%20Customer_1.jpeg?width=670&height=293&name=Purchase%20Report%20Customer_1.jpeg)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/purchase-order-summary-report_

- Accessing the purchase order report

### Purpose

The Purchase Order Summary Report allows you to quickly view all details related to the Purchase Orders for a specific customer.

### Accessing the Purchase Order Report

Accessing the Purchase Order Report can be done in two ways:

1. Type "Purchase Order Report" in the search bar at the top of the page. A link to the page will appear and can then be clicked.
2. Manually navigating through the menu at the top of the page. Go to Reports > Purchase Order Report.

### How to run the Purchase Order Report

- Select the customer you wish to generate the report for from the search bar.
- Fill in the fields using the below descriptions **Field**
**Description**

Order By

Date Added - The date the Purchase order was entered into CartonCloud.
Arrival Date - The date the stock within the Purchase Order arrived into the warehouse.

Purchase Order History Status

Verified - Search for Purchase Orders which have arrived but
where the stock is not yet allocated to a warehouse space.
Allocated - Search for Purchase Orders where the stock
has arrived and has already been allocated to a warehouse space.

Date Range
To find Purchase orders that arrived into the warehouse during a specified time period.
- Click Show Report and the requested report will be generated at the bottom of the screen.
- Alternatively, the report can be exported to an Excel file. Click Export Excel and the report will download in the backrgound. You will be notified once the report is ready with the bell notification in the top right corner. Example Report:

<a id="rate-card-report"></a>
## Rate Card Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/rate-card-report_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Exporting a Transport Rate Card Report
  - Cascading rates
  - Example page
- Exporting a Warehouse Rate Card Report
  - How to run the report
  - What the report displays
  - Example page

### Purpose

Please note that if your CartonCloud account was created prior to 1 July 2019 the below functionality may not be available at this stage. If you would like to discuss further, please use [CartonCloud Help](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) and lodge a case with our Service Desk.

The Rate Card Report allows you to extract your Warehouse and Transport Rates from CartonCloud into easy-to-read files. You can export rates based on the Customer or the Rate Card itself.

- Transport Rate Card Report can be exported as a PDF
- Warehouse Rate Card Report can be exported as a PDF or Excel file

### Exporting a Transport Rate Card Report (PDF)

Please note that if you have a WMS Only CartonCloud account, you will not have access to Exporting a Transport Rate Card Report

- Navigate to Reports > Rate Card Report .
- Select a Customer or a Rate Card to run the report off.

#### ![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Apr-22-2026-06-23-30-5012-AM.png?width=3420&height=826&name=image-png-Apr-22-2026-06-23-30-5012-AM.png)

- If you wish to specify only certain rates to be exported , use the filters provided.
- Select Export PDF .

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Apr-22-2026-06-25-02-9147-AM.png?width=3420&height=1458&name=image-png-Apr-22-2026-06-25-02-9147-AM.png)

#### Cascading Rates

If you have cascading rates set up against a rate card then the secondary Rate Card will be included in the Rate Schedule. It will appear underneath the Rate Card you have selected. The cascaded rates title will appear at the top left of the page to allow you to identify when the schedule changes from listing rates from one Rate Card to another.

#### Example Transport Rate Card report output

The below page is an example of what the Rate Card Report will look like once generated for a Customer. Please note the Logo, Address and other company information will populate based on what you have set up within your [Organisation Settings](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Organisation+Settings)(so your company's logo will appear instead).

![Rate Card Report_4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Rate%20Card%20Report_4.avif)

### Exporting a Warehouse Rate Card Report (PDF or Excel)

Please note that if you have a TMS Only CartonCloud account, you will not have access to Exporting a Warehouse Rate Card Report

You can export a complete WMS Rate Card — covering all charge sections — as a

PDF

or

Excel

file directly from the Rate Card Report page.

#### How to run the report

- Select the **Customer**or **Rate Card** you wish to run the Report for
- For PDF, click Export Rate Card PDF
- For Excel, click the down arrow and Export Rate Card Excel

As these are WMS Rates the Status, Service Type, Zone and Date filters are not relevant, and do not effect the output of the exported file

#### What the report displays

The Warehouse Rate Card displays all Rates and Settings from the following tabs of the relevant Rate Card:

- Details
- Adhoc Charges
- Storage Charges
- Handling Charges

#### Example page (PDF)

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Apr-17-2026-06-10-28-3571-AM.png?width=521&height=660&name=image-png-Apr-17-2026-06-10-28-3571-AM.png)

CartonCloud has a number of Reports that can be run and downloaded within the application. In addition there are three reports than can be set up to be run on a daily schedule as outlined below [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com#scheduled-reports).

- Discrepancy Report
- Purchase Order Summary Report
- Sale Order Report
- Stock Movement Report
- Customer Stock Report
- Bulk Export Purchase Orders
- Bulk Export Sale Orders
- Consignment Report
- Consignment Invoice Report
- Bulk Export Manifests
- Rate Card Report
- Stats
- Automation Report
- Usage Report

- API Client Usage Report

Scheduled Reports run:

To set up a scheduled report, head to the Customer Settings and follow our guide on [Outgoing Notification Emails](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Configuring-Outgoing-Notification-Emails-to-Customers)

| **Report Name** | **Description** | **Scheduled Time** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Stock Notification](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Customer-Settings-Email-Notifications) | Stock Warning / Expiry Notification Email | 8:00am AEST Mon-Fri |
| [Consignment Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Consignment-Report) | Customisable daily Consignment Activity | 5:00am AEST Tues-Sat |
| [Sale Order Summary Report](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Sale-Order-Report) | Daily Sale Order Report | 5:00pm AEST Mon-Fri |

<a id="sale-order-report"></a>
## Sale Order Report

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-order-report_

### Table of Contents

- Report overview
- How to navigate to the report
- How to run the report
- Viewing options

### Report overview

The Sale Order Summary Report provides you with a list of all Sales Order data. The Sale Order Summary Report can be used to analyse Sale Order data and sales performance within a particular time frame. The Report can be ordered by Address or Pack Date and then filtered by Date Packed, Date Added or Date Dispatched. You also have the option to include Sale Order Custom Fields, Delivery/Packing Instructions and Comments. In addition, you can use templates when running your reports to save having to manually select the columns you wish to include each time you access the report.

![sale-order-report-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-0.png?width=670&height=246&name=sale-order-report-0.png)

### How to navigate to the report

To access the Sale Order Report select **Reports** in the main menu followed by **Sale Order Report** in the drop-down menu.

### How to run the report

- Select the Customer you wish to run the report for.
- Select how you wish to order the report by either Address (the delivery address of the Sale Order) or Pack Date (date the order was packed) .
- Select the Date Filter.
  - Date Packed or Date Added: Packed Date is only respected when a date value is set for to and from. When no date is set, both Date Packed and Date Added are respected.
  - Date Packed: the date the Sale Order was packed
  - Date Added: the date the Sale Order was added to CartonCloud
  - Dispatched Date: the date the Sale Order was dispatched
- Select the Sale Order History Status to include in the report.
  - All statuses
  - All Processed (Dispatched, Packed)
  - Draft
  - Rejected
  - Awaiting Pick and Pack
  - Packing in Progress
  - Packed
  - Dispatched
- Select the From and To date to run the report for.
- Select the Columns you wish to include in the report. Search for a column in the column window or click +Add All Columns to include all columns.
- You can choose to save the report configuration as a Report Template or use an existing template. See Creating Report Templates for more information.

If you run a report with the status Draft, Rejected, Awaiting Pick and Pack, or Packing in Progress (and don't include the status of Dispatched or Packed) you have the option to run the report with no Pack Dates. If you **do** run the report with **no Pack Dates** this may cause the report to take some time to run.

If you select a status that has orders which do not have Pack Dates**,**the report may result in no data being returned. This will also be reflected in any reports you export.

### Viewing options

Once you have selected your report configuration you can choose how you wish to view the report:

**Show Report**

Selecting this option will return the list of Sales Orders on the screen

![sale-order-report-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-1.png?width=670&height=280&name=sale-order-report-1.png)
**Export Excel**

Selecting this option, your report will run in the background
![sale-order-report-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-2.png?width=560&height=58&name=sale-order-report-2.png)

You will be notified once the report is ready by the bell in the top left of the screen
![sale-order-report-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-3.png?width=400&height=117&name=sale-order-report-3.png)

You can then download the file and view in Excel.

**Example Report**

![sale-order-report-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-4.png?width=670&height=66&name=sale-order-report-4.png)

---

## Sale Order Report (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/sale-order-report-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Where to access the sale order report
- Report overview
- How to run the report
- Viewing options

### Where to access the Sale Order Report

To access the Sale Order Report select **Reports** in the main menu followed by **Sale Order Report** in the drop-down menu.

### Report Overview

The Sale Order Summary Report provides you with a list of all Sales Order data. The Sale Order Summary Report can be used to analyse Sale Order data and sales performance within a particular time frame. The Report can be ordered by Address or Pack Date and then filtered by Date Packed, Date Added or Date Dispatched. You also have the option to include Sale Order Custom Fields, Delivery/Packing Instructions and Comments. In addition, you can use templates when running your reports to save having to manually select the columns you wish to include each time you access the report.

![sale-order-report-customer-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-customer-0.png?width=670&height=246&name=sale-order-report-customer-0.png)

### How to run the report

- Select the Customer you wish to run the report for.
- Select how you wish to order the report by either Address (the delivery address of the Sale Order) or Pack Date (date the order was packed) .
- Select the Date Filter.
  - Date Packed or Date Added: Packed Date is only respected when a date value is set for to and from. When no date is set, both Date Packed and Date Added are respected.
  - Date Packed: the date the Sale Order was packed
  - Date Added: the date the Sale Order was added to CartonCloud
  - Dispatched Date: the date the Sale Order was dispatched
- Select the Sale Order History Status to include in the report.
  - All statuses
  - All Processed (Dispatched, Packed)
  - Draft
  - Rejected
  - Awaiting Pick and Pack
  - Packing in Progress
  - Packed
  - Dispatched
- Select the From and To date to run the report for.
- Select the Columns you wish to include in the report. Search for a column in the column window or click +Add All Columns to include all columns.
- You can choose to save the report configuration as a Report Template or use an existing template. See Creating Report Templates for more information.

If you run a report with the status Draft, Rejected, Awaiting Pick and Pack, or Packing in Progress (and don't include the status of Dispatched or Packed) you have the option to run the report with no Pack Dates. If you **do** run the report with **no Pack Dates** this may cause the report to take some time to run.

If you select a status that has orders which do not have Pack Dates**,**the report may result in no data being returned. This will also be reflected in any reports you export.

### Viewing options

Once you have selected your report configuration you can choose how you wish to view the report:

**Show Report**

Selecting this option will return the list of Sales Orders on the screen

![sale-order-report-customer-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-customer-1.png?width=670&height=280&name=sale-order-report-customer-1.png)

 **Export Excel**

Selecting this option, your report will run in the background
![sale-order-report-customer-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-customer-2.png?width=560&height=58&name=sale-order-report-customer-2.png)

You will be notified once the report is ready by the bell in the top left of the screen
![sale-order-report-customer-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-customer-3.png?width=400&height=117&name=sale-order-report-customer-3.png)

You can then download the file and view in Excel.

**Example Report**

![sale-order-report-customer-4](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/sale-order-report-customer-4.png?width=670&height=66&name=sale-order-report-customer-4.png)
