# Account Management > Users

<a id="adding-removing-customer-access-to-user-profiles"></a>
## Adding/Removing Customer access to User Profiles

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-removing-customer-access-to-user-profiles_

- In some instances, you may have a user that requires access to multiple customers that have been set up in CartonCloud.
- To make changes to a users profile follow the steps below.
- Select Customers in the main menu, followed by Users in the drop-down menu.
- Then select Edit .
- By clicking into the Customer Box, you can now add or remove the accessible customer's access as required.
- Also, check if charging information should or shouldn't be visible.

- Select Save and the changed will be applied immediately.
- If a user has access to multiple customer's they will now be able to select them as shown in the animation below (the top option is the selected tenancy, the bottom option is the selected Customer within that tenancy).

---

<a id="adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles"></a>
## Adding/Removing Warehouses to User Profiles

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to modify the warehouses a user has access to

### Purpose

In some cases, you may need to add or remove warehouses to a user's access. To do so, you can edit the user and add or remove warehouses to their profile.

### How to modify the warehouses a user has access to

- Navigate to the Users page, Contacts > Users .
- Select the relevant User.
- Select the blue Edit button.
- Scroll down to the Warehouses section.
- Select the Warehouses you wish to give the user access to and/or unselect the Warehouses you want to remove from the user's access.
- Scroll to the bottom of the page and select Save .

![adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles-0.png?width=670&height=156&name=adding-removing-warehouses-to-user-profiles-0.png)

<a id="bulk-importing-users"></a>
## Bulk Importing Users

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/bulk-importing-users_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to import users in bulk

### Purpose

To import Users in bulk.

### How to import users in bulk

- Navigate to the Users page, **Contacts**>**Users**.
- Select **More** and then **Import CSV**.

![bulk-importing-users-0](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-importing-users-0.png?width=447&height=106&name=bulk-importing-users-0.png)

- Select **Download Sample Data**.

![bulk-importing-users-1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-importing-users-1.png?width=446&height=209&name=bulk-importing-users-1.png)

- Open the downloaded file and edit accordingly using the below table as a guide. Column Header

Description

Detail

Name

User Name

Email

User Email Address

Create

Create User Now

Yes
No

Password

User Password

Roles

Roles - if assigning more than one role then separate each with a semi-colon.

Administrator;Packer;Customer;Data Entry;Onforwarder; Driver

Customers

If creating a 'Customer' type user you need to type the relevant Customer Name in. Note, these are the Customers to which the User will have access. If assigning more than one role then separate each with a semi-colon.

Where User is of type 'Customer'

Warehouses

The warehouses the user will have access to. If assigning more than one role then separate each with a semi-colon.
- Save the file.
- Navigate back to CartonCloud and select **Choose file**.
- Select the relevant file.
- Click **Upload File**.

![bulk-importing-users-2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-importing-users-2.png?width=670&height=314&name=bulk-importing-users-2.png)

- A success message will appear. If you selected Yes for Create User Now you will see their password on this page. Ensure you select the Download List of Generated Passwords option.

![bulk-importing-users-3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/bulk-importing-users-3.png?width=670&height=89&name=bulk-importing-users-3.png)

If you need to hide charging information from the created Users you will need to manually select each newly created user and enable this setting.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/Zm1z94iyE4g

<a id="creating-or-inviting-new-users"></a>
## Creating or Inviting New Users

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/creating-or-inviting-new-users_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to invite/create a new user
- Additional settings
- User role specific settings
- Accepting a CartonCloud user invitation
- Troubleshooting

### Purpose

For someone to access CartonCloud they need to be created or invited as a User first.

Follow along Vincent as he steps through how to add a new User to your CartonCloud account.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/NxMJZ6zhI08

How to invite/create a new User

- Navigate to the Users page (Contacts>Users).
- Click on **+Invite New User**. The below screen will appear.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-or-inviting-new-users-0-png.png?width=510&height=681&name=creating-or-inviting-new-users-0-png.png)

- Fill in the name and email field with the user's details.

It is recommended that for staff who do not have their own email address that you select the Create User option and use a placeholder email instead (the email is only used as login details).

- You have two options when generating a new User, you can either **invite** or **create** the User.  To create a user tick the **Create User Now** box.
  - **Invite User:** select this option if you wish to send an email invitation to the user and have them create their own password. This option is best for Customers and staff with Administrator access.
  - **Create User:**selectthis option if you wish to create the user immediately and set up their password on their behalf. This option is best for internal staff such as Packers and Drivers.
- Fill in the remaining fields using the below field descriptions.

| **Field** | **Field Description** |
| --- | --- |
| **Additional Settings** | Provides the option to hide all charging information from this user. |
| **Create User Now** | Tick the box next to **Create User Now** if you wish to **create** the user rather than invite them.  Invite user: do not tick this box if you wish to invite the user.  Create user: tick the box to create the user and password immediately. If **Create User Now** is ticked an extra option **Generate Password Automatically**will appear. This will automatically set a password up for the user and display it on the screen upon submitting the form. |
| **Email** | **Invite user:** this is where the invitation will be sent. Upon accepting the email the user can then change the email address if they wish. **Create user:**if the user does not have an email address, a placeholder email can be utilised instead. |
| **Roles** | Select the Roles you wish to enable for the user. There is no limit to the number of roles a user can have. A brief overview of each role is provided on the page. For more information on each role see [User Roles Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/User-Roles-Explained). Note, if you would like the user to have access to the mobile application, the Packer or Driver role must be ticked. |
| **Subscribe** | If you wish the user to be subscribed to CartonCloud Newsletters. We recommend leaving this ticked so the User will receive important product updates related to CartonCloud. They are able to unsubscribe at any time if they wish. |
| **Warehouses** | Tick the applicable warehouses the user will be operating within. See [Setting up Warehouses (Multiple Sites)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Setting-up-Warehouses-Multiple-SitesSetting-up-Warehouses-Multiple-Sites)  for more information. |

### Additional Settings

For each user, you have the option to hide all charging information. This includes:

- The Charges tab will be hidden on Sale Orders, Purchase Orders and Consignments
- Rate Cards will not be visible.
- Invoices will not be visible.

### User Role Specific Settings

Some User Roles have specific settings that you can choose to apply.

| **User Role** | **Setting** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Driver | List user on summary sheets even if they have no delivery runs to do | When enabled, the driver will appear on summary sheets regardless of whether they have delivery runs to complete. |
| Driver | Automatically Emal Run Sheets to Driver | When enabled, the driver will be emailed their Run Sheets automatically. |
| Driver | Enable this Driver to Add or Edit Consignment Items via the Mobile Device | When enabled, the driver will have the ability to add and edit Consignment Items from the mobile app.  **Setting options:** **Use Organisation Settings:**will apply the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level. **Enabled:**regardless of the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level, the driver will be able to add and edit Consignment Items via the mobile app.  **Disabled:** regardless of the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level, the driver will NOT be able to add and edit Consignment Items via the mobile app. Please see [Add/edit Consignment Items for Drivers on the Mobile App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Add-edit-Consignment-Items-for-Drivers-on-the-Mobile-App) for more information. |
| Administrator | Allow this user to edit other users | When enabled the user will be able to edit other users.  If the user has this permission enabled it will appear as Yes on the Users list view screen under the heading 'Can edit users'. |
| Administrator | Allow access to the BI Dashboard | *This setting is only available if the user has 'Allow this user to edit other users' enabled.* This will give the user access to the [Business Intelligence Tool](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Business) if the account has the BI Dashboard enabled. The BI Dashboard is a paid add-on feature.  Note, that [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) accounts will have access to unlimited BI Dashboard users, however, **for non-WMS Premium accounts** **additional users will be an additional cost.**Please reach out to our [Service Desk](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket)team if you have any questions. |
| Onforwarder | Carrier(s) | Choose which Carriers the user will have access to. |

### Accepting a CartonCloud User Invitation

If needed, new users can get assistance with accepting their invitation from the video below.

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/pn0iPdU7e1g

What to do if the user accepts the invite but cannot seem to access the Tenancy or Customer

One thing to keep in mind is that a CartonCloud User has a single login to view all the tenancies (3PL warehouses) and customers they have access to.

This means if you invite them to your tenancy they will need to manually select to view your tenancy from the drop-down menu.

If a user you have invited is reporting not being able to access your Tenancy or Customer. Please first ask them to double-check they have attempted to select it in the drop-down menus shown below.

![creating-or-inviting-new-users-1-png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/creating-or-inviting-new-users-1-png.gif?width=398&height=164&name=creating-or-inviting-new-users-1-png.gif)

- The top drop-down menu allows the user to move between tenancies.
- The bottom drop-down menu allows the user to move between Customers within those tenancies.

### Troubleshooting

It's very common for invitation emails to end up in spam or junk folders, so it's always a good idea to have the User check those locations as well for their invitation.

**What to do if the user accepts the invite but cannot seem to access the Tenancy or Customer:**

- One thing to keep in mind is that a CartonCloud User has a single login to view all the tenancies (3PL warehouses) and customers they have access to.
- This means if you invite them to your tenancy they will need to manually select to view your tenancy from the drop-down menu.
- If a user you have invited is reporting not being able to access your Tenancy or Customer. Please first ask them to double-check they have attempted to select it in the drop-down menus shown below.
- The top drop-down menu allows the user to move between tenancies.
- The bottom drop-down menu allows the user to move between Customers within those tenancies.

**What to do if the user is deactivated due to an unverified email address:**

CartonCloud automatically deactivates users whose email addresses remain unverified after account creation. This is a security measure to ensure only verified users can access the system.

- To resolve this issue: ✅ **Email verification must be completed to prevent automatic deactivation in the future.**
  - **Re-enable the user account (You may need to reach out to [CartonCloud Support](https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/new-support-ticket) to re-enable the User)**:
    - Navigate to **Contacts > Users**.
    - Use the **Filters** to locate the deactivated user.
    - Click **Edit** next to the user and set **Active** to **Yes**.
    - Click **Save**.
  - **Ask the user to verify their email**:
    - Once the user is re-enabled, they need to log in.
    - Direct them to **Settings** at:
[https://app.cartoncloud.com/settings](https://app.cartoncloud.com/settings)
    - From their **Settings** page, they can complete the **email verification** process.

---

<a id="disabling-users"></a>
## Disabling Users

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/disabling-users_

Please note, you must have permission to edit other users to be able to disable a user. To have this permission you must have administrator access. See [User Roles Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/User-Roles-Explained)for more information.

Once a CartonCloud user has been created it cannot be deleted, however, it can be disabled. This is because CartonCloud Users may have access to multiple CartonCloud Organisations (tenancies). When disabling them from within your account they can still log in to CartonCloud, but can no longer access your Organisation.

- To deactivate a user, in the Main Menu click on Contacts , then click on Users in the drop-down menu.
- Next, find the User you want to disable and select them.
- Finally, click Disable User .

The animation below demonstrates how to disable and re-enable a User.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/disabling-users-0-png.gif?width=1852&height=1208&name=disabling-users-0-png.gif)

Once a user is disabled you will not see them in the All tab. Instead, you will need to use the Filter tab and select Inactive to Yes, then click Go!

---

<a id="drivers"></a>
## Drivers

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/drivers_

### Table of Contents

- What is a Driver?
- How to create a Driver
- Driver List View
- View Driver
  - Details
  - Run Sheets
  - Cash on Deliveries
  - Consignments & Statistics
  - Optimise Map
  - Location History

### What is a Driver?

A Driver in CartonCloud had access to the mobile app to complete deliveries and the web app to view their assigned Consignments and Run Sheets.

### How to create a Driver

To create a new Driver follow the [Setting up Drivers in CartonCloud](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Setting-up-Drivers-in-CartonCloud) article.

### Driver List View

The Driver's page provides a full list of all active drivers within your Organisation. An active driver is a driver that has had a Consignment allocated to them during that week (including deleted ones).

From the Driver's page you can see which drivers are currently online (indicated by a green or red circle next to their name) and if they have location services enabled (indicated by a green or red pin next to their name).

![image-png-Mar-03-2026-01-55-19-0377-AM](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/image-png-Mar-03-2026-01-55-19-0377-AM.png?width=670&height=152&name=image-png-Mar-03-2026-01-55-19-0377-AM.png)

### View Driver

By selecting a driver you are able to view and edit that Driver's details. The below describes what options and features are available from each tab on the View Driver screen.

#### Details Tab

To view the relevant details of the Driver, including:

- Driver: the driver's name.
- Email: the driver's email.
- Online: if the driver is online.
- Location Access Available: If the driver had enabled location access.

#### Run Sheets Tab

The Run Sheets assigned to the Driver.

You can email the Run Sheets to the Driver using the **Email Run Sheets to Driver** button.

#### Cash On Deliveries Tab

The  [Cash on Deliveries](https://help.cartoncloud.com/articles/Knowledge/Cash-on-Deliveries) associated with the Driver.

#### Consignments & Statistics Tab

The Consignments assigned with the Driver.

The statistics for the Driver are summarised in a table showing the **Total Consignments**, **Total Completed** and**Total Incomplete**.

#### Optimise Map

Optimise the route of the driver according to the Consignments allocated to the driver.

![](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/drivers-1-png.png?width=670&height=352&name=drivers-1-png.png)

#### Location History

The location history of the driver.

---

<a id="edit-user"></a>
## Edit User

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/edit-user_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- How to edit a user
- Additional settings
- User role specific settings

### Purpose

The edit User page allows you to update an already existing User's information and permissions.

### How to Edit a User

Note, to be able to edit a User you need the 'Allow this User to edit other users' enabled against your own user. This will need to be enabled by someone with this permission.

- Navigate to the Users page, Contacts>Users.
- Select the User you wish to edit.
- Click Edit .

![edit-user-0-png](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/edit-user-0-png.png?width=670&height=262&name=edit-user-0-png.png)

- Edit the fields using the below field descriptions as a guide.
- Select Save.

![Edit_User_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hubfs/Edit_User_2.avif)

| **Name** | The user's full name |
| --- | --- |
| **Email** | The User's contact email. This is where the invite will be sent to. If you invite rather than create the User, the User will be able to change this themselves when they accept the invitation. |
| **Password** | Change the User's password. |
| **Warehouses** | These are the warehouse the User will have access to. |
| **Roles** | The roles assigned to the User. This will dictate what information and functionality the User will have access to. For more information please see [User Roles Explained](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/User+Roles+Explained) |
| **Additional Settings** | Provides the option to hide all charging information from this user. |
| **Subscribe** | We recommend leaving this ticked so the User will receive important product updates related to CartonCloud. They are able to unsubscribe at any time if they wish. |

### Additional Settings

For each user, you have the option to hide all charging information. This includes:

- The Charges tab will be hidden on Sale Orders, Purchase Orders and Consignments
- Rate Cards will not be visible.
- Invoices will not be visible.

### User Role Specific Settings

Some User Roles have specific settings that you can choose to apply.

| **User Role** | **Setting** | **Explanation** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Adminstrator | Allow this User to edit other Users | Give access to the Admin user to edit other Users. |
| Adminstrator | Allow access to the BI Dashboard | *This setting is only available if the user has 'Allow this user to edit other users' enabled.* This will give the user access to the [Business Intelligence Tool](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Business) if the account has the BI Dashboard enabled. The BI Dashboard is a paid add-on feature.  Note, that [WMS Premium](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/WMS-Premium) accounts will have access to unlimited BI Dashboard users, however, **for non-WMS Premium accounts** **additional users will be an additional cost.**Please reach out to our [Service Desk](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/contactsupport)team if you have any questions. |
| Driver | List user on summary sheets even if they have no delivery runs to do | When enabled, the driver will appear on summary sheets regardless of whether they have delivery runs to complete. |
| Driver | Automatically Email Run Sheets to Driver | When enabled, the driver will be emailed their Run Sheets automatically. |
| Driver | Enable this Driver to Add or Edit Consignment Items via the Mobile Device | When enabled, the driver will have the ability to add and edit Consignment Items from the mobile app.  **Setting options:** **Use Organisation Settings:**will apply the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level. **Enabled:**regardless of the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level, the driver will be able to add and edit Consignment Items via the mobile app.  **Disabled:** regardless of the settings configured at the Organisation Settings level, the driver will NOT be able to add and edit Consignment Items via the mobile app. **Please see [Add/edit Consignment Items for Drivers on the Mobile App](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=577767258) for more information.** |
| Onforwarder | Carrier(s) | Choose which Carriers the Onforwarder will have access to. |

<a id="overview-of-cartoncloud-s-user-interface"></a>
## Overview of CartonCloud's User Interface

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/overview-of-cartoncloud-s-user-interface_

### Table of Contents

- User Interface Video Overview
- Search for anything!

Becoming familiar with CartonCloud's interface will help in ensuring a smooth onboarding process. As you use CartonCloud more, naturally you will become more familiar with the user interface, however, until then you can use the below video to assist you in the initial stages of using CartonCloud.

### User Interface Video Overview

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/UzWd5BpYFlQ

### Search for anything!

In CartonCloud, you can use our global search tool to search for anything. This means Menu's, references and much more. Some examples of this include; Consignments, Sale Orders, Purchase Orders and Addresses.

The Search for Anything bar is only visible to Administrator and Customer Users.

The Search Box appears up the top next to your Organisation name:

![User Interface_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/User%20Interface_1.jpeg?width=670&height=38&name=User%20Interface_1.jpeg)

**Refine your Results:**
You can also refine your search to a particular 'type', using keywords:

Address
Consignment
Customer
Delivery
Delivery Run
Manifest
Product
Purchase Order
Sale Order
User
Warehouse Location

For example, to search Consignments going to IGA Burleigh Heads:
"Consignment IGA Burleigh Heads "

<a id="setting-up-drivers-in-cartoncloud"></a>
## Setting up Drivers in CartonCloud

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/setting-up-drivers-in-cartoncloud_

For a driver to use CartonCloud (including the Mobile App) they must be set up as a User.

To set up a driver as a user, please follow the [Creating or Inviting New Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/display/KB2/Creating+or+Inviting+New+Users) article, ensuring you tick the Driver role within it.

Once completed, the Driver can then login to the Web App via the website [https://app.cartoncloud.com](https://app.cartoncloud.com.au/)  or login to the Mobile App by downloading it through the Apple App Store (iPhone) or Google Play Store (Android). We will cover CartonCloud Driver training in a future section.

This also now allows you to allocate Consignments to Drivers. Steps on how to allocate will also be covered in future sections of this guide.

It is also possible to allocate consignments on a Delivery Run automatically to a Driver upon the Consignments creation.

Next Step: [Setting up Vehicles in CartonCloud (optional)](https://help.cartoncloud.com/pages/viewpage.action?pageId=530055403)

---

<a id="user-modes"></a>
## User Modes

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/user-modes_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Relevant user roles
- Limits
- Choose user mode
- Switch user mode

### Purpose

The CartonCloud mobile app offers two user modes, "Delivering" and "Picking". Depending on what roles a user has been assigned via the CartonCloud web app, one or both of these user modes may be available.

### Relevant user roles

- Driver
- Packer

These user roles are assigned to each user within the CartonCloud web app by a system administrator. To be able to log into the CartonCloud mobile app at least one of these roles must have been assigned to you. Should you only have one role assigned to you, you will not be presented with all of the options to choose or switch your user mode mentioned below. You will simply be operating in your assigned space (e.g. Packers will not have the *Delivering*option unless they are also a Driver).

### Limits

Each user role does come with some limitations in regards to what functionality is accessible within the app while you are operating in the corresponding user mode.

For example, while in "Picking" mode you will not be able to optimise routes, allocate jobs or collect PODs. Similarly, while in "Delivering" mode you won't be able to pack Sale Orders.

### Choose user mode

Upon logging into the CartonCloud app you will be presented with a dialogue allowing you to choose the initial user mode you want to be operating in. If you choose to cancel this view, the default selection of "Delivering" will be applied (or Picking if you do not have Driver privileges).

Should you only have been assigned a Driver role, you will not be given an option to choose your user mode but will be directly forwarded to the appropriate user mode (*Delivering*).

![User Mode_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/User%20Mode_1.jpeg?width=195&height=386&name=User%20Mode_1.jpeg)

### Switch user mode

To switch the current user mode, open the main slide-in menu and choose "Switch Mode". This will then open a view with user-mode options. Select the save button (blue ticks in the top right corner) to confirm your selection and update the app content accordingly.

Should you only have been assigned one user role, you will not have the option to switch the current user mode.

![User Mode_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/User%20Mode_2.jpeg?width=229&height=450&name=User%20Mode_2.jpeg)

---

<a id="user-roles-explained"></a>
## User Roles Explained

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/user-roles-explained_

### Table of Contents

- User roles explained
- Additional settings
- User roles web or mobile access

### User roles explained

When you create a User, you can select the role you wish to assign to them. This role will determine what access they have within your CartonCloud account. The below describes the different roles a user can be assigned to.

| Administrator | Selecting this option provides access to all areas within CartonCloud, however there is an additional settings that can restrict this user. When you select the Administrator role tick box there is an option that appears to allow this user to add and edit other Users. If this is not selected the user will not have the ability to add or edit other users and their settings. This is typically only enabled for the System Administrator within your organisation for CartonCloud. |
| --- | --- |
| Customer | This role restricts the user to only login as a specific Customer. Please note that Order entry screens and features are different and restricted for these users. Note you must select at least one Customer. Note if you wish to provide a user with Administrator role access to login as a customer they will be provided with a drop down when the login to select which Customer they wish to emulate. |
| Data Entry | This role provides the user with the ability to add, edit and view consignments, Manifests and upload consignment invoices (hard copy POD's & other paperwork). As a data entry user if you add documents to a Consignment it then needs to be approved by an admin user before the document is uploaded. |
| Driver | Select this role for all users who need to login to the mobile app for Delivering and to login to the Web App to view their Consignments and Run Sheets. You can assign one or more Carriers to a Driver user. When a Carrier is assigned, the Driver is only visible to Onforwarder users who share the same Carrier — Onforwarders cannot allocate consignments, Run Sheets, or Delivery Runs to Drivers outside their assigned Carriers. |
| Onforwarder | Enable this role for external Onforwarders who need to login to the system to update consignment status, attach additional paperwork and view their allocated consignments. Choose which Carriers the Onforwarder will have access to. |
| Packer | Select this option for users who need to view, edit and pack Purchase Orders and Sales Orders. This is also required for users who wish to use the mobile app for Putaway, Picking and Wave Picking features |

As a guide, the following user types would have these roles selected.

| User Type | Administrator | Packer | Customer | Driver | Data Entry | Onforwarder |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| System Admin | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |
| Operations | Yes |  |  |  |  |  |
| Driver |  |  |  | Yes |  |  |
| Administration | Yes |  |  |  |  |  |
| Warehouse Manager | Yes | Yes |  |  |  |  |
| Customer Service |  |  |  |  | Yes |  |
| Onforwarder/ Subcontractor |  |  |  |  |  | Yes |
| Customer |  |  | Yes |  |  |  |
| Warehouse Picker |  | Yes |  |  |  |  |

### Additional settings

For each user, you have the option to hide all charging information. This includes:

- The Charges tab will be hidden on Sale Orders, Purchase Orders and Consignments
- Rate Cards will not be visible.
- Invoices will not be visible.

### User Roles Web or Mobile Access

Below shows the various user roles and which interface that user role can access.

![User Roles Explained_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/User%20Roles%20Explained_1.jpeg?width=344&height=348&name=User%20Roles%20Explained_1.jpeg)

<a id="users"></a>
## Users

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/users_

### Table of Contents

- What is a user?
- Benefits
- Adding a new user
- Users list view page
- View user

### What is a user?

A user in CartonCloud is an individual who will have access to your CartonCloud account with differing levels of access and control.

When you create a User, you can select the role you wish to assign to them. This role will determine what access they have within your CartonCloud account. For more information on User Roles, click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/User-Roles-Explained).

### Benefits

- Allows you to cater to a variety of staff members with different functions and responsibilities.
- It gives your staff autonomy to make changes and access data in CartonCloud themselves.
- Drivers will be able to do their job efficiently as they will only see the assigned jobs.
- It gives limited access to your Customers, allowing them to place and see their orders without emailing you but preventing them from seeing other Customers information.

### Adding a New User

To create a new User, see the [Creating or Inviting New Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Creating-or-Inviting-New-Users) page.

### Users List View Page

On the main Users page, you can search for a User, export and import users and add new users.

![Users_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Users_1.jpeg?width=670&height=152&name=Users_1.jpeg)

### View User

To view an existing User simply click on the User on the User List View page. For information regarding the View User page click [here](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/View-User).

---

<a id="users-customer"></a>
## Users (Customer)

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/users-customer_

### Table of Contents

- Inviting another user from the company
- Accepting the invite

### Inviting another user from the company

From this page it is possible to get another user the same level of access you have to CartonCloud, this means you can give another employer access to creating orders without needing them to use your login.

- To invite a user begin by selecting the Actions button, then select Invite New User.
- Enter the new users details ensuring the email address is correct and then click Continue .

![UsersCustomers_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/UsersCustomers_1.jpeg?width=582&height=198&name=UsersCustomers_1.jpeg)

- A window will pop up allowing you to customise the invite message the User will receive (this is a great time to send them any additional instructions)

![UsersCustomers_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/UsersCustomers_2.jpeg?width=407&height=401&name=UsersCustomers_2.jpeg)

- Once you are happy with the message select Send Invite and the email will be sent off.

### Accepting the invite

**📹 Video:** https://www.youtube.com/embed/pn0iPdU7e1g

What do if the user accepts the invite but cannot seem to access the Tenancy or Customer

One thing to keep in mind is that a CartonCloud User has a single login to view all the tenancies (3PL warehouses) and customers they have access to.

This means if you invite them to your tenancy they will need to manually select to view your tenancy from the drop-down menu.

If a User you have invited is reporting not being able to access your Tenancy or Customer portal. Please first ask them to double-check they have attempted to select it in the drop-down menus shown below.

![UsersCustomers_3](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/UsersCustomers_3.jpeg?width=488&height=201&name=UsersCustomers_3.jpeg)

- The top drop-down menu allows the User to move between tenancies.
- The bottom drop-down menu allows the User to move between Customers within those tenancies.

<a id="view-user"></a>
## View User

_Source: https://help.cartoncloud.com/knowledge/view-user_

### Table of Contents

- Purpose
- Edit the user
- Disable the user
- Associate address and/or delivery run to a user

### Purpose

On the View User page, you can edit and disable the User and associate an address and delivery run to the User.

![View user_1](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/View%20user_1.jpeg?width=670&height=301&name=View%20user_1.jpeg)

### Edit the User

**To edit the User:**

- Select the blue Edit button.
- For more information on editing a User click here .

### Disable the User

See [Disabling Users](https://help.cartoncloud.com/help/s/article/Disabling-Users) for steps on how to disable a User.

### Associate Address and/or Delivery Run to a User

**Associate an Address to the User**

Associating an address to a User is mainly designed for Drivers. Once you have linked an address to the Driver it will appear on their mobile application when they are optimising their route. This is useful for the Driver's home address as when optimising the route it will take into consideration that the driver either wants to begin and/or end their delivery route at home.

![View User_2](https://help.cartoncloud.com/hs-fs/hubfs/View%20User_2.jpeg?width=265&height=455&name=View%20User_2.jpeg)

**To associate an address to the User:**

- Select the Addresses tab.
- Click **+Link New Address**.

**Associate a Delivery Run to the User**

By associating a Delivery Run to a particular User it grants the User access to viewing the Delivery Run.

**To associate a Delivery Run to a User:**

- On the details tab of the User, click**Edit Delivery Runs**.
- Click **Add Delivery Run**.
- Select the Delivery Run from the drop-down menu.
- Click **Save Changes**.
